prAk.h chetanatvAdityanena trayaH prayogAssUchitAH | pitAputrau nopAdAnopAdeyabhUtau chetanatvAddevadattayaj~nadattavat.h | putrAdyachetano, na pitrAdichetanopAdAnakaH, achetanatvAt.h ghaTavat.h | putrAdichetano na pitrAdyachetanepAdAnakaH, chetanatvAdbrahmava(hmAdiva)diti | sarvatra pakShadharmatAyAshcha nishchitatvAt.h | dvitIye tAvadvayAptimupapAdayati- na chetanavikAraH syAditi ||
yadi khalu yatra kvApi deshe kAle vA.achetanaM chetanavikAro dR^iShyaH syAttadaivaM vyAptirbhajyeta | nachaivamityarthaH | mahadAdijagat.h brahmakAryamupalabdhamiti chenna | adyApyasiddheH | uktavakShyamANapramANairnirAkR^itatvAt.h(cha) | tR^itIye vyAptimupapAdayati- nAchetaneti ||
vyAkhyAnaM pUrvavat.h | evaM na chetanavikArashchetano.apyupalabdha ityAdye.api vyAptirupapAdanIyA | 
athavA mahadAdikaM na chetanavikAraH, achetanatvAdghaTavaditi yuktyantaraviruddhaM cha brahmaNo jagadupAdAnatvamiti chetasi nidhAyAsya vyAptimupapAdayati- na chetaneti || nanu ghaTAdayo.api brahmavikArA iti chenna | mR^idAdivikAratvasya pramitatvAt.h | paramparayeti chet.h | evaM tarhi na svayaM chetanavikArAH | kintu tatkAraNAnItyuktaM syAt.h | tathAcha kathaM na dR^iShyAntatA | tarhi tatkAraNeShu vyabhichAra iti chenna | teShAmeva pakShatvAt.h | sukhaduHkhAdiShvanaikAntikatvamiti chenna | teShAmantaHkaraNavikAratvAbhyupagamAt.h | etenaitadapi pratyuktam.h | jagat.h, abhinnanimittopAdAnam.h prekShApUrvajanitakAryatvAtsukhAdivaditi | ghaTAdiShu vyabhichAra(rAchcha)shcha | teShAmapi pakShIkaraNe pramANabAdhaH syAt.h | nanvachetanamapi jagachchetanavikArashchettadA ko doShaH syAt.h | evaM tarhi chetano.apyachetanavikAraH syAt.h H na chaitadastItyAha- nAchetaneti ||
ayamabhisandhiH | yadi mahadAdikaM brahmaNo vikAraH syAttarhitatsvarUpAnugatimatprasajyeta | kArye kAraNasvarUpAnugamadarshanAt.h | ghaTAdayo mR^idvikArA mR^idanugatimanto dR^iShyAH | na chaitadasti | tasmAnna mahAdAdi(H) brahmavikAraH | yadi punaH kAraNasvarUpAnugamamantareNa vikArivikArabhAvo.abhyupagamyate tadA chetano.apyachetanavikAraH kiM nAbhyupagantavyaH | nachaivamaN^gIkR^itaM pareNa | tathAhi sati "eka AtmanaH sharIre bhAvAt.h' ityatra parasya bhUtachatuShyayapariNAma evAyaM chetanavAnkAya iti vadantaM chArvAkaM prati bhUteShvavidyamAnaM chaitanyaM kathaM kArye syAditi parihAro madirAdravye madashaktivatsyAditi punashcha chArvAkeNa chodite madiropAdAne.api sUkShmarUpamadashaktivyutpAdanaM cha vyAhataM syAditi | 
yadvA brahmajagatI nopAdAnopAdeyabhAvavatI vilakShaNatvAddevadattaghaTavat.h | nanu vilakShaNAnAmapi mR^idghaTAdInAmupAdAnopAdeyabhAvo dR^ishyata iti chenna | chetanAchetanarUpavailakShaNyasya vivakShitatvAt.h |
api cheti yuktisamuchchaye | vikR^iti(ta)tve vikR^itidashAyAmanyasyAnyarUpatvamanyavikAratvaM na dR^ishyate | vikAravikAriNAvanyonyamanyatayA kvApi nopalabdhAviti yAvat.h | atra dR^iShyAntamAha- neti ||
yasya kShIrasya vikAro yaddadhi tasmAtkShIrAdanyatA tasya dadhnaH kenApi kvApi na dR^ishyata ityarthaH | evamanyatAdarshanasya siddhA vikAravikAribhAvAdvayAvR^ittiH | tataH kimityata Aha- sarvaj~nAditi ||
hishabdo yasmAdityarthe | tasmAnna tayorvikAravikAribhAva iti sheShaH | ayamatra prayogaH | jagat.h brahmavikAro na bhavati 
tato.anyatvenopalabhyamAnatvAt.h | yo yato.anyatvenopalabhyate na sa tadvikAro yathA ghaTaH paTasya | yashcha yadvikAro nAsau tato.anyatvenopalabhyate, yathA dadhi kShIrAditi |
yadvA jagadbrahmaNI nAnyonyavikAravikAriNI | anyonyamanyatvenopalabhyamAnatvAt.h | ghaTapaTavaditi prayogaH | nachAyamasiddho hetuH, yaH savarj~na iti brahmaNaH sarvaj~natvashravaNAt.h | j~nAnakAryasya sarvathA.apyanupalambhena jagato j~nAnAbhAvAnumAnAt.h | viruddhadharmAdhikaraNayoshchAnyonyamanyatvopalambhaniyamAditi bhAvenoktam.h- sarvaj~nAditi || nanu vikAravikAriNorbhedAbhyupagamAt.h kathamayaM heturiti chenna, bhedenaivopalambhasya hetutvAt.h | tatkiM tvadabhyupagamamAtreNa ghaTapaTayorabhedaH, utopalambhAt.h | nAdyaH, madabhyupagamena shuddhabhedasyaiva grAhyatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | asiddheH | abhedAnupalambho vA hetutvena vivakShitaH | 
nanvayamasiddho hetuH | jagat.h brahmaNA.abhinnaM sattvAdbrahmavadityanumAnenAbhedopalambhAditi che(t.h)nna | kharvaM svarNenAbhinnaM, sattvAtsvaNarvadityAbhAsamAnayogakShematvAdityAha- abheda iti ||
yadi jagadbrahmaNoH sAdhyeta tarhIti sheShaH | kharvam.h ayaH kharparaM vA | nanvidamiShyameva | kharvasuvarNayorabhedasya mayA.aN^gIkR^itatvAditi chenna | abhedashabdena bhedAbhAvasya vivakShitatvAt.h | atra pramANavirodha iti chet.h | jagat.h brahmaNo.atyantaM bhidyate tatsvarUpAnugama(ti)shUnyatvAditi, tvadanumAnasyApi, pramANavirodha itrata samaM samAdhAnam.h | atyantabhedo mama na kvApItyaprasiddhavisheShaNateti chenna | mokShAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | tathAhi | j~nAnena nivR^ittakarmaNA cha mokSho.abhyupeyase | ta(chcha)tra j~nAnamaj~nAnamapi bhavati | nivR^ittaM karma pravR^ittamapi bhavatIti kathaM mokShasAdhanaM syAt.h | j~nAnatvAdinA tadbhAve.aj~nAnAderapi (tadbhAvaH) tathAtvaM syAt.h | j~nAnAdikaM j~nAnAdisvarUpeNAtyantAbhinnam.h aj~nAnAdisvarUpeNa(tu)bhinnAbhinnamato na kAryasaN^kara iti chet.h | tathA.apyaj~nAnAdyabhedena svakAryasya kartavyatvAt.h | evaM mokSho.api saMsArAbhinna ityamokShassyAt.h | mokShAtmatA(nA)sadbhAvena mokShatve saMsAro.api tathA syAt.h | yadi vA(chA)yamabhedo.anupalabhyamAno.arthakriyAsu nopayujyate, tadA vyasanitayaivAbhyupagantavyaH syAditi |
brahmasvarUpAnugatishUnyatvAnna tatpariNAmo.ayaM prapaJNcha ityuktam.h | tatra kiM sarvasvarUpAnugatishUnyatA.abhipretA, uta kiJNchidanugamashUnyatA | nAdyaH | sarvAnugamAbhAve.api ghaTAdInAM mR^idAdivikAratvadasharnAt.h | na dvitIyaH, sattvAnugamena vikAravikAribhAvopapatterityata Aha- abheda iti || abhedo vikAravikAribhAvaH | 
nanu na suvarNagataM sattvaM kharve.anugatam.h | tatkathaM(ayaM)prasaN^gaH | tatkiM brahmasattvameva viyadAdInAm.h | addheti chenna, pramANAbhAvAt.h | "prANA vai satyaM teShAmeva satyam.h' ityAdishruteH prANasatyatvasya brahmAdhInatArthatvopapatteH | brahmaNa eva sAmAnyasattA viyadAdAvanugateti chettarhi kathaM na svarNasattA kharve.anugatA | 
atha manyase kAraNameva kAryAtmanA bhavatIti pariNAmavAdinAM matam.h | tatashcha kAraNaM yatsvabhAvAvyabhichAri tadanugamaH kArye.avashyAbhyupagantavyaH | anyathA kAraNameva kAryAtmanA bhavatIti riktaM vachaH syAt.h | avyabhicharitasvabhAvAnanugame kAraNasyaivAnanugamaprApteH | nacha sanmAtrasvabhAvaM suvarNam.h | yena kharvaM tadvikAraH syAt.h | kintu tadavyabhichArisuvarNatvAdyanugame satIti | evaM tarhi jagadapi kathaM brahmapariNAmaH syAt.h | nahi sanmAtrasvabhAvaM brahma | kintu vij~nAnamAnandaM brahmetyAdishrutyA vij~nAnAdInAmapi tadavyabhichArisvabhAvatvAvagamAt.h | nacha vij~nAnAnandAdyanugamaH prapaJNche.astIti samam.h | 
nanu cha kShIrAvyabhichArisvabhAvamAdhuryAnugatividhuraM dadhi tadvikAro dR^iShyamiti chenna | satkAryavAdabhaN^gaprasaN^gAt.h | kiJNcha kShIrakAryaM dadhIti nishchaye na mAdhuryaM kShIrasvabhAva iti kalpyate | mAdhuryasya kShIrasvabhAvatAnishchaye vA kShIravinAshe tatkAraNasya dadhyupAdAnatvaM kalpyata sati na doShaH | api chAgamairanumAnaishcha brahmaNo nirvikAratve siddhe sati aprachyutasvarUpasvabhAvasyaiva (brahmaNo) jagadupAdAnatvaM yo manyate taM pratyetau prasaN^gaviparyayAvuktAviti ko virodhaH | etena pradhAnasya jagadupAdanatve.apyayaM samAno doSha iti nirastam.h | 
atha matam.h | dvirUpaM brahmAbhyupagamyate anantAnandachidAtmakaM sadAtmakaM cheti | tatrAdyena rUpeNa nimittam.h | dvitIyenopAdAnam.h | ato na kashchidukto doShaH | tathAhi | yattAvaduktaM nirvikAratvaM tachchichChaktiviShayatvAchChatyAderadUShaNam.h | nimittakAraNena chichChaktikena prakR^itipradhAnAdyabhidhAnaM sachChaktikaM brahma pariNamatItyaN^gIkAre na yuktivirodho.api sadAtmakasya jagadupAdAnatvAchchaitanyAdyananugame.api na doShaH | sadanugamasya vidyamAnatvAt.h | anyatvadarshanaM cha na viruddhayate sarvaj~nAt.h, tannimittameva nopAdAnam.h | yachchopAdAnaM sadrUpaM tasmAdbhedenopalabhyata ityAshaN^kayAha- bhogeneti ||
yadi brahmaNaH pariNAmaH chidbhAgena nirvikAratvamaN^gIkriyate, tadA vaktavyam.h, tayorbhogayorabhedo bhedAbhedau vA | na tAvadabhedaH 
dvayorapi pariNAmitvAdiprAptyA bhAgAdvayakalpanAvaiyarthyAt.h | nApi bhedAbhedau, abhedena saN^karaprasaN^gAt.h | bhedo.abhedakAryaM niruNaddhIti chet.h | kiM tarhyaprayojakenAbhedena, tasmAdbhAgayoratyantabheda evAN^gIkaraNIyaH | 
tataH kimityata Aha- yo bhAga iti ||
parasparamatyantAbhinne dve vastunI | tatraikaM nirvikAraM jagannimittameva | aparaM tu pariNAmi jagadupAdAnatamevetyaN^gIkAre neshvarasya kevalanimittatvavAdinAmasmAkaM kashchidvivAdaH | nirvikArasya jagannimittasyAsmAbhirIshvaratvena, pariNAmino jagadupAdAnasya pradhAnatvena svIkR^itatvAt.h | vivAdAbhAvAchcha prakR^itishcheti(tyAdi)sUtrANAmanArambha eveti | atra yo bhAga iti parAbhyupagamenoktam.h | svamatena tu yadvastviti j~nAtavyam.h | nahi bhAgina vinA bhAgaH sambhavati | nApi vikAryavikAriNoH kashchidbhAgI vidyate | 
nanvasti vivAdaviShayaH | nimittopAdAnabhedavAdinA nimittasyaiva brahmatvamabhyupagamyate | mayA tu sadanantAnandachitAM samudAyasyeti tadarthamadhikaraNArambha iti chet.h | kimidaM brahmatvam.h | (kiM) brahmanAmavatvamuta jagatkAraNatvAdilakShaNArtha(vat.h)tvam.h | AdyaM dUShayati- bhinnAnAmiti ||
tadbhavedityabhyupagamamAha | tatashchAyamarthaH | yadyarthe na vivAdo.asti tadA.anArambhaNIyamevAdhikaraNam.h | shabdamAtre pareNa vivAdAkaraNAt.h | karaNe.apyashabdashAstratvAditi | 
dvitIye.api vivektavyam.h | kiM parasparaM bhinnAH sachchidAnandAdyAH pratyekaM brahmANi | uta te na brahmANi kintu tatsamudAya eveti | nAdyaH | ekamevAdvitIyamityAdishrutivirodhAt.h | dvitIye.api tatsamudAyo nAma kiM tadupAdAnakaM dravyAntaraM saN^khayA vA saMyogo vA | sarvatrApi doShamAha- brahmeti |
tadeti | manasi sthitAnAM vikalpitAnAM pakShANAM (vA)aN^gIkAre | kvachitpakShe | hishabdenAnupapatteH prasiddhatAmAha | atra hi brahmopAdAnasya vA tadguNino vA jagadupAdAnatvaM prAptamiti vishvasya brahmopAdAnakatA na syAt.h | na hyupAdAnaguNigatAH shaktayaH kAryadravye guNe vA sambhavanti | tadupAdAnatvAderasambhavAt.h | 
athavA brahmaNaH kAryatvAdguNatvAchcha na vishvopAdAnatvaM sambhavatIti vyAkhyeyam.h | atra brahmopAdAnatetyupalakShaNam.h | brahmanimittakatA cha na yuktetyapi draShyavyam.h | 
syAdetat.h | kAlAtyayApadiShyametadanumAnajAtam.h | "yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante' "Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH' "janmAdyasya yataH' itayAdivirodhAt.h | "janikartuH prakR^itiH' iti prakR^itAvupAdAnalakShaNAyAM hi paJNchamI vidhIyate | tathA chaivodAhR^itam.h | "R^iN^gAchCharo jAyate, gomayAd.h vR^ishchiko jAyate' iti | prasiddhashchAtropAdAnopAdeyabhAva iti | tadidamasaN^gatam.h | paJNchamIbalAtkilopAdAnatvaM siShAdhayiShitam.h | nachedaM sUtramupAdAne paJNchamyA vidhAyakam.h |
atha matam.h | apAdAne tAvatpaJNchamI vihitA | apAdAne paJNchamIti | upAdAnaM chApAdAnavisheShaH | janikartuH prakR^itiriti smaraNAt.h | tato.apAdAne vihitA paJNchamyupAdAne.api bhaviShyati | nachaivaM sati paJNchamyA niyamenopAdAnatvAsiddhiH | visheShasmaraNasya grAhyatvAdityata Aha- R^iN^gAditi |
tathAshabdo dvitIyodAharaNena sambaddhayate | evamAdyeShUdAharaNeShu R^iN^gAdInAM sharAdInpratyapAdAnatvamiShyate | paJNchamyarthatayeti sheShaH | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | sUtre chetyapi j~nAtavyam.h | 
etaduktaM bhavati | bhevedevaM kathaJNchidyadi sUtra(sya)tadudAharaNAnAM(cha) paraparikalpito.artho bhavet.h | na chaivam.h | kiM nAma janikartuH prakR^itirityanenedamuchyate | janeH kartujarAyamAnasya yA prakR^itirupAdAnasaMsR^iShyamapAyAvadhibhUtaM dravyaM tatkArakamapAdAnasaMj~naM bhavatIti | udAharaNeShvapi yachChR^iN^gAdInAM sharAdInpratyapAyAvadhitvameva paJNchamIpratipAdyamiti |
etadeva prapaJNchayati- upAdAneti ||
yadyapyatra R^iN^gAdau sharAdyupAdAnabhUtaikadeshavattvaM pratIyate | tathA.api yA.atrApAdAnatA apAyAvadhitvalakShaNA.asti saiva brahmaNo dR^iShyAnto bhavet.h | paJNchamyarthatAyAmudAharaNaM bhavet.h na tUpAdAnatetyarthaH | ayamabhiprAyaH | R^iN^gAdikaM hyekadeshena sharAdInpratyupAdAnamekadeshena chApAyAvadhitayA kArakaM bhavati | tasminnasatyekadeshAntarasyopAdAnatA.anupapatteH | mudgamAShAdayo hi yadyapi tuShAntarAvasthitenaivAMshenAN^kuropAdAnam.h | tathA.api na tuShavikAlAnAmuptA(maMshA)nAmaN^kurajanakatA.asti | tatrAvadhibhAga evApAdAnaM paJNchamIvAchyashcha | tad.hdR^iShyAntena brahmaNo.api paJNchamIbalAdupAdAnapradhAnasaMsR^iShyAvadhitvameva bhavati | na tUpAdAnatvamiti | nanu kathaM tarhi prakR^itermahAnmato.ahaN^kAra ityAdiprayogaH | tatrApi pariNatabhAgasaMsR^iShyasya apariNatabhAgasya 
avadhibhUtasya paJNchamIviShayatvamiti vadAmaH | yatra sarvasyApi pariNAmastatrakatham.h | na prayoktavyaiva tatra paJNchamI | nahi kShIrAddadhi jAtimiti prayuJNjate | kintu kShIrameva dadhi jAtamiti | yatra kvachitprayogo dR^ishyate sa gauNo vA sUtrasyArthAntarakalpanAmUlo veti |  Vyasa-(4)
atha manyeta | R^iN^gameva sharopAdAnam.h | natu kechidavayavA upAdAnaM kechittadavadhaya iti vibhAgaH | tathA sati R^iN^gAchCharo jAyata iti prayogAnupapatteH | yadi cheyaM paJNchamyupAdAne yadi vA.avadhau tathA.api R^iN^gAvayavAditi vaktavyam.h | nacha tarhi avadhitvamevAstu iti vAchyam.h | nirupAdAnotpattiprasaN^gAt.h | ataH R^iN^gasyaivopAdanatvAttatra paJNchamIshravaNAdupAdAne paJNchamIti | tatrAha- na hIti ||
atra R^iN^gAdAvupAdAnate(taiye)ti na vaktavyam.h | apariNatabhAgasya sharAN^kurAderatyantabhinnasya pramitatvAt.h | anyathedamasyopAdAnamidaM neti vyavasthAnupapatteriti hishabdArthaH | kathaM tarhi R^iN^gAditi prayoga ityata Aha- bAhyAvayaveti ||
bAhyAH sharAkAreNa pariNatebhyo.anye ye.avadhibhUtAvayavAsteShAM gauravAdbahutvAt.h | 
etaduktaM bhavati | katipayAvayaveShu pariNateShucha bahUnAmavashiShyatvena R^iN^gAntarotpattyA R^iN^gabuddhimAtrotpattyA vA R^iN^gashabdopapattiriti |
nanu kutaH sUtrAderarthAntarakalpanA | shabdArthavirodhAditi brUmaH | upAdIyate kAryamanena svarUpatayA svIkriyata ityupAdAnam.h | apAdIyate parityajyate kAryamanenetyapAdAnam.h iti sphuTo vipratiShedhaH | 
kiJNcha bhAShyakAreNAyamapi yogaH shakyo.avaktumiti pratyAchakShANenAyameva sUtrArthaH sUchitaH | yadi tarhi janikartuH prakR^itiriti sUtramupAdAnasyApAdAnasaMj~nA vidadhyAt.h | kathaM tarhi dhruvamapAye.apAdAnamityanenaiva gatArthatAmAha | na hyapAdAnasyApAye dhruvatvamiti | tasmAduchapAdAnasaMsR^iShyasyaivAvadhibhAgasyApAdAnasaMj~nAyAmanena vihitAyAM bhAShyakArIyaM dUShaNaM sambadhyate | tathA sUtraM samAdadhAnairapi tasyaivAyaM prapaJNcha ityuktam.h | anyathA prAgavadherapAdAnasaMj~noktA | atra tUpAdAnasya | na hyavadhirupAdAnamityeko.athar ityavakShyan.h | atasteShAmapi sammato.ayamartha iti gamyate | 
astu vopAdAne.api paJNchamI | tathA.api (yata iti) paJNchamIbalAdupAdAnatvanishchayo nopapadyate | anekArthatvAt.h | visheShasmaraNAdityuktamiti chet.h | kimidaM visheShasmaraNAt.h | janidhAtugrahaNeneti chet.h | tarhyAtmana AkAshaH sambhUta ityAdInAmanudAharaNIyatvaM syAt.h | kutashcha yata iti paJNchamItyavadhR^itam.h | taseH sArvavibhaktikatvAt.h | Atmana AkAsha satyanenaikArthatvAditi chenna, tasyAH paJNchamyAM "bhuvaH prabhavaH' iti visheShAvi(vakShi)hitAbhivyaktyavadhitArthatvAt.h | tathA chaivodAhR^itam.h | himavato gaN^gA prabhavati prathamamupalabhyata ityathar ityAstAM vistaraH | 
athavA yaduktaM na brahmavikAro vishvaM tato bhedenopalambhAditi | tadasat.h | sharAdiShu vyabhichArAt.h | sharAdayo hi R^iN^gAdayo hi R^iN^gAdyupAdAnAstatA bhedenopAdAnAstato bhedenopalabhyanta ityato gUDhAbhisandhirAha- R^iN^gAditi ||
evamAdyeShu sthaleShu sharAdInprati R^iN^gAdInAma(pya)pAyAvadhitvalakShaNamapAdAnatvameveShyate | na punarupAdAnatvam.h | ato vipakShatvAbhAvAdbhedenopalambho na tatra sAdhyaM vyabhicharatIti | nanu kathamuchyate R^iN^gAdInAM sharAdInprati nopAdAnatvamiti | tathA satyupAdAnAntarAnupalambhAchCharAdInAM nirupAdanotpattiH prasajyetetyato.abhisandhimudghATayati- upAdAneti ||
R^iN^gAderuktarUpApAdAnatve.api nacha sharAdInAM nirupAdAnatvoktiprasaN^gaH | katipayAnAM R^iN^gAdyavayavAnAM sharAdyupAdAnatvAbhyupagamAt.h | nachaivamanaikAntyatAdavasthyam.h | yadyapyatra R^iN^gAdau sharAdyupAdAnaikadeshatvaM pra(tI)dR^ishyate | tathA.apyatra R^iN^gAdau yasyaikadeshasyoktasya rUpApAdAnatA sa eva brahmaNo dR^iShyAnto bhavet.h | tata eva sharAdInAM bhedopalambhAt.h | na tUpAdAnabhAgaH | tatastadabhAvAt.h | 
etaduktaM bhavati | R^iN^gAderavayavA hi kechichCharAdInAmupAdAnabhUtAH kechinnimittabhUtAH | tatra ye nimittabhUtAsteShu hetuvR^ittAvapi nAnaikAntyam.h | teShAM sapakShapraviShyatvAt.h | ye tUpAdAnabhUtAsteShAM vipakShapraveshe.api na tatra hetuvR^ittiriti kuto.anaikAntyamiti | 
yastu vaiyAtyAnmanyate | nAtrApAdAnatA.asti | kintUpAdAnatvameva kevalam.h | tathA chAnaikAntikatvamiti | sa praShyavyaH | kimatrAvinaShya eva R^iN^gAvayavyupAdAnamityabhiprAyaH, kiM vA R^iN^ge.avinaShye tadavayavAH sarve.apIti, uta naShye R^iN^ge tadavayavAH sarve.apIti | 
nAdya ityAha- nahIti || atra R^iN^ge | tathAtve suvarNavachChare R^iN^gasyApi pratItiprasaN^gAditi hishabdArthaH | 
na dvitIya ityAha- nahIti || avinaShyR^iN^geShu tadavayaveShu sarveShu sharAdyupAdAnataiveti na yuktam.h | tathA sati R^iN^gasharayoH samAnadeshatAprasaN^gAditi hishabdena sUchayati | 
na tR^itIya ityAha- nahIti || atra sarveShvapi R^iN^gAvayaveShu R^iN^ganAshottaraM sharAdyupAdAnataiveti na yujyate | ato nAnaikAntyamiti hishabdaH | kuto na yujyata ityata Aha- bAhyeti || kAryAdbAhyAnAmapariNatAnAmavayavAnAmupalambhAt.h | apariNatasyApyupAdAnatve.atiprasaN^gAt.h | 
nanu R^iN^gaM chennaShyaM kathaM tarhi sharotpattyanantaramapi R^iN^gapratyayaprayogAvityato gauravAdityuktam.h | samAdhAnaM pUrvavat.h | mA bhUdbhedopalambhasyAtra vyabhichAraH | tathA.api yaduktaM nAchetanavikArashchetana iti tadatra vyabhicharati | achetanAdgomayAdeH chetanasya vR^ishchikAderjananadarshanAdityata Aha- nacheti ||
tatra gomayAdervR^ishchikAdijanmani | nanvanAdishchetana iti pUrvAbhyastAhArAbhilAShAdinA prasiddham.h | anyathA pUrvakarmAbhAve janmano.apyasambhavAt.h | madhye kathaJNchitsambhave.apyAdisarge sarvathA(api) anupapatteH | tatkathaM nirdalamidamAshaN^kitam.h | satyam.h | tathA.api pareNa svagranthe niveshitatvAt.h | achetanAchchetanasya janmAbhAve gomayAd.h vR^ishchiko jAyata ityAdivyavahAravirodha ityata Aha- upAdAnatayeti ||
pUrveNaiva sambandhaH | na vayaM kAraNatvamAtraM niShedhAmo yena vyavahAravirodhaH syAt.h | kintUpAdAnatayA | tasyaiva prakR^itatvAt.h |

asya vR^ishchikAdishabdAbhidheyasya | pradR^ishyate hIti tato nirgatatvopalambhAdityarthaH | nanvekadeshenApAdAnatvamabhyupagatamiti | satyam.h | tachCharIrApekShayetyuktam.h- kAryadehagatasyeti ||
gomayAdyupAdAnakadehagatasyetyarthaH |

evaM brahmaNo jagadupAdAnatvAbhAve pramANAnyabhidhAya paropanyAstAni pramANAni nirAkariShyan.h kramasyAprayojakatvapariNAmAditi sUtrArthatayoktAM shrutiM tAvannirAchaShye- sachcheti ||
"sachcha tyachchAbhavat.h niruktaM chAniruktaM cha nilayanaM chAnilayanaM cha vij~nAnaM chAvij~nAnaM cha satyaM chAnR^itaM cha satyamabhavat.h' ityasyAM shrutAvasya brahmaNaH sattyadAdishabdAbhidheyamUrtAmUrtArAshidvayAtmakavishvabhAva uchyata iti nAsti | kuto netyata Aha- tatsR^iShTveti ||
"sa idaM sarvamasR^ijata | yadidaM kiJNcha | tatsR^iShTvA tadevAnuprAvishat.h | tadanupravishya | sachcha tyachchAbhavat.h' iti vachanena brahmaNaH sattyadAdibhavanAtpUrvamevAsya mUrtAmUrtarUpasya vishvasyotpatteravagatatvAt.h | etaduktaM bhavati | nedaM sattyadAdibhavanaM vishvo(syoshva)tpAdAnAt.h | vishvotpattyuttarakAlInatvAt.h | yA kriyA yaduttarakAlInA, nAsAvasau | yathA bhuktvA charatItyuktaM charaNaM na pUrvakAlInaM bhojanamiti | anupapannArthaM chAnyathA vAkyamApadyeta | nahi mR^itsuvarNAdikaM ghaTaruchakAdi sR^iShTvA tadanupravishya tadbhavati |

kastarhi shrutyartha ityata Aha- sattvAditi ||
jagadbhAvaM vinA sattvAdidharmayogena brahmaiva tathA sattyadAdikamuchyate | tarhi tadanupravishyetyasyAnvayo nAsti | nahi brahmaNaH sattvAdidharmayoge sadAdishabdavAchyatve vA jagatpraveshasyopayogo.asti | nApi tataH pUrvakAlInatA | kiJNchaivaM sati prasiddhivirodhaH sattyadAdishabdAnAM "dve vA va brahmaNo rUpe' ityAdau mUrtAmUrtavAchitayA prasiddhatvAt.h ityato jagadgatena rUpeNetyuktam.h | yadyapyananyApekShayA sarvadA sattvAdidharmayogaH sadAdishabdavAchyatA cha brahmaNaH | tathA.api tattadvastugatarUpeNaiva tattachChabdavAchyatvamityasti vyavasthA | tathAcha mUrtAmUrtajagadgatena rUpeNa brahmasadAdishabdavAchyamityataH tadanupravishyeti sambaddhayate | parameshvarasannidhAnAdeva mUrtAmUrtAderapi sadAdishabdavAchyatA chopapadyata iti |
sattvAduttamatvAtsat.h | tatervyAptestyat.h | tanu vistAra ityasmAD.hDyat.hpratyayaH | vaidikatvAnniruktam.h | nishchayenoktaM hi niruktam.h | nahi vedAdR^ite.anyena brahma nishchayena vaktuM shakyate | samyagvastumashakyatvato.aniruktam.h | yadyapi nishchayenoktaM na 
bhavatItyaniruktam.h | tathA.api niruktamityanena virodhAtsamyak.h kAtsnaryena vaktumashakyatvata ityuktam.h | nanu vedetarapramANenAniruktamiti kuto na vyAkhyAyate | na | prakR^itaparityAgaprasaN^gAt.h | vedena niruktamiti (hi) prakR^itam.h | kiJNchokteH shabdadharmatvAtpratyakShAnumAnAbhyAmaniruktamityayuktam.h | smR^itInAmapi vedAtmakatvena virodhatAdavasthyam.h | mahimAdhikyaM chAtra labhyata iti | jagadAshrayatvAnnilayanam.h | nishchitamayante pravartante.asminniti | ro la iti yogavibhAgAllatvam.h | nipUrvasya lI(N^.h)shleShaNa ityasya vA.adhikaraNe lyuTi kR^ite rUpametat.h | svAshrayatvAdanilayanam.h | na vidyate svAtiriktaM nilayanaM yasyeti | j~nAnatvAdvisheShaj~nAnarUpatvAdvij~nAnam.h | durvidatvato durj~neyatvAdavij~nAnam.h | na vidyate vij~nAnaM sakalavisheShAvagAhijIvaj~nAnaM yadviShaya iti | sattateH samyagvyApteryAtAnAdyatanaM prati hetutvAchcha satyam.h | tanoteH D.hvipratyaye takAramAtraM rUpam.h | tena sachChabdasya bahuvrIhiH | yatI prayatna ityasyAntarNItaNyarthasya Dapratyaye (yamiti) rUpam.h | tataH karmadhArayaH | "ayasmAyadIni Chandasi' iti bhasaMj~nAshrayaNAjjashtvAbhAvaH | durjanairaprApyatvAdevAnR^itaJNcha | natu mithyAtvAt.h | yadyapi R^itaM prAptaM netyanR^itam.h | tathA.api "brahmavidApnoti param.h' ityAdishrutivirodhaparihArAya durjanairityuktam.h | hishabdo brahmaNo mithyAtvAbhAve prasiddhiM dyotayati | nityasAdhuguNavyAptiyantR^irUpatvataH satyam.h | atra nityatvata ityekaM vyAkhyAnam.h | nityasatyashabdayoraikAthyarsya vakShyamANatvAt.h | sat.h sAdhuguNAH "sadbhAve sAdhubhAve cha' iti | vachanAt.h teShAM vyAptirbAhulyaM takAreNoktam.h | pUrvavattanoterbhAve D.hvipratyayaH | tasya yantR^irUpatvAdyam.h | yama uparama iti dhAtoH (ityato) DaH | bhakteShu sAdhuguNabAhulyaprerakatvAditi yAvat.h | abhavaditi vachanAdbrahmaNaH sattvAdikaM sAdIti shaN^kAnirAsAyoktam.h- sadeti || pratyekaM chAsya sambandhaH | 
tarhi kathamabhavaditi prayoga ityata Aha- vyaktiriti ||
uktaguNAnAM sadAdishabdokta(ktAnAM)dharmANAM vyaktiH pratItiH | nR^iNAmupadeShyR^ipuruShApekShayA sR^iShyau satyAveva bhavet.h hi yasmA(dasmA)tkAraNAt.h | atra cha nityaguNe.api brahmaNi sadAdikamabhavaditiprayogo yujyate | tatashchAyaM shrutyarthaH sampadyate | tat.h brahma mUrtAmUrtAtmakaM vishvaM sR^iShTvA tatprerakatvena nAnArUpaistadeva vishvaM pravishya prAk.h sR^iShyerupadeShyR^INAmupadeshyAnAM cha sharIrendriyavatAmabhAvAdapratItaguNakaM sat.h athedAnImupadeShyR^INAmupadeshyAnAM cha shaNIrendriyavattve sati pratItasattvAdiguNamabhavaditi | tadanena pArameshvarI sR^iShyiryogyAnAM svaguNaj~nAnArthetyuktaM bhavati | yathoktam.h | "so.ayaM vihAra iha me tanubhR^itsvabhAvasambhUtaye bhavati bhUtikR^ideva bhUtyAH' iti |
brahmapariNAmanirAkaraNamupasaMharati- tasmAditi ||
nirvikAra evAsheShakarteti sambandhaH | dvibhAgaM brahmeti yannirAkR^itaM tasyopasaMhAra eka iti | pariNAmAnupapattAvuktayukteranuvAdo vA | ato na brahmopAdAnatvaM prakR^ityadhikaraNArtha iti (sambandhaH) sheShaH | kastarhi tadartha ityata Aha- shabdairiti ||
ityarthosyeti sheShaH | anenApavyAkhyAnanirAkaraNasya svavyAkhyAnadArDhyArthatvAt.h nAsaN^gatirityapi sUchitam.h | 
nanu vaktavyArthasyAvashiShyatvAtkathamupasaMhAraH kriyate | tathAhi | pratij~nAdR^iShyAntAnuparodhAdityuktaM tAvaddUShaNIyam.h | satyam.h | vivartanirAkaraNena nirAkariShyate | tarhyabhidhyopadeshAchchetyatroktaM "bahu syAM prajAyeya' iti vAkyaM dUShaNIyamiti chenna | asyApi sachcha tyachcha' iti vAkyavyAkhyAnanyAyenaiva vyAkhyAtatvAdityAha- bahu syAmiti ||
tasyaiva nirvikArasyaiva | uktamArgeNetyasya (eva)vivaraNaM tattadgatena rUpeNeti || 
tattadanantapadArthaprerakAnantarUpairbahu syAmiti so.akAmayatetyasyAH shruterartha ityarthaH | 
evaM tarhi "sa idaM sarvamasR^ijata' ityuttaravAkyamasaN^gataM syAt.h | na hyanyArthaM saN^kalpamabhidhAyAnyakriyAbhidhAnaM saN^gachChate | nahIshvaro.asvatantro.asatyakAmo vetyata Aha- tadarthamiti || 
tattatpadArthaniyAmakabahusvarUpatvakAmanAnantaraM niyamyApekShatvAt.h niyAmakatvasya, tadarthaM niyAmakabahusvarUpatvArthaM, niyamyaM jagattAvadasR^ijat.h, tato niyAmakabahusvarUpo bhUtvA, tadevAnuprAvishaditi, vAkyayojanopapatteH kAtrAsaN^gatirityarthaH | anenaiva "tadAtmAnaM svayamakuruteti' shrutirvyAkhyAtA veditavyA | na hyatrAtmAnaM prapaJNchAtmanA.akuruteti shrUyate | ubhayAmnAnaM cha UrNanAbhidR^iShyAntAktyaiva nirastam.h | nahyUrNanAbherutpadyamAnasya, tasminneva lIyamAnasya cha, tantorUrNanAbhirupAdAnam.h | kintu tadupabhuktamannamevetyuktam.h | yonishchetyetatprAgeva nirastamiti yukta evopasaMhAra iti |

brahma vishvAtmanA dR^ishyata iti yat.h, sa sarga iti kathyata ityetAvatpariNAmavAde.api samam.h | ata uktamavikR^itameveti | 
avikR^itatvaM kuta ityata uktamekamiti | advitIyam.h | niravayavaM chetyarthaH | 
tathAhi | kiM brahmaNaH svata eva vishvAkArapariNAmaH | kiM vA parataH | nAdyaH, kvApyadarshanAt.h | yadapi kShIravaddhItyudAhR^itam.h | tat.h kAlAdervidyamAnatvAdayuktam.h | svechChayaiveti chenna | prayojanAbhAvAt.h | svabhAvo.ayamiti chenna | prekShAvattvahAneH | na dvitIyaH | advitIyatvAt.h | nacha niravayavaM kvApi pariNataM dR^iShyam.h | AkAshaM saMyogAdimadupalabdhamiti chenna | dravyAkAraNapariNAmasya prakR^itatvAt.h | paramANvAdayastu svarUpeNaiva na siddhA iti | 
avikR^itamevAnyadanyAtmanA dR^ishyata ityasambhavi ityata uktam.h- mR^iSheti || mR^iShAshabdena vishvasya brahmatAdAtmyasya taddarshanasya chAnirvachanIyatochyate | yathA rajjuravikR^itaiva mR^iShA bhujaN^gAdyAkAreNAbhAsate tathaiveti | tarhi vishvopAdAnamanyadvaktavyamityata uktaM mandadR^iShyayaiveti | mandA bhavati dR^iShyiryayA sA mandadR^iShyistayA mAyayetyarthaH | athavA.asambhavaparihArArthamuktaM mandadR^iShyayaiveti | mandA chAsau dR^iShyishcha mandadR^iShyirbhrAntistayetyarthaH | bhrAnterapi yAthArthyAdvishva(sya)satyatApattirityata uktam.h- mR^iSheti || tadetanmithyAprapaJNchAropAdhiShThAnatvameva brahmaNaH prakR^itishchetyAdinA kathyata iti |

dUShayitumupakramate- kathyata iti || yad.h brahma vivartavAdinA kathyate, tasya dUShaNaM kathyata, ityAvR^ittyA yojanIyam.h | tachcha neti naJNanuvR^ittirvA kartavyA | kuto netyato vikalpena pR^ichChati- seti ||
vishvasya brahmavivartatve nirAkartavye mandadR^iShyayAshrayaprashno.anupapanna ityata uktam.h- seti || ekasya tachvAprachyutasya pUvarviparItAsatyAnekarUpAvabhAsalakShaNavivartatayA, tadupAdAnatayA, choktetyarthaH | mandadR^iShyAvAshrayAnirUpaNAdinA nirAkR^itAyAM sarvamidaM nirAkR^itaM bhavatIti bhAvaH | tasyaiva, yadavaShyambho vishvo vivarta, ityarthaH | tato.anyagA jIvagatetyarthaH | kiMshabdasyobhayataH sambandhaH | 
mAyAvAdino hi kechit.h brahmaiva svAvidyayA jagadAkAreNa vivartate svapnAdivaditi manyante | bimbasthAnIyaM brahma mAyAshaktimat.h kAraNaM, jIvAshcha pratyekamavidyA.anubaddhAH, ityapare | mAyA.avidyApratibimbitaM brahma jagatkAraNam.h, viruddhaM cha brahmAbhUtatvAlambanaM jIvAshchAvidyA.anubaddhA ityanye | jIvA eva svAvidyayA pratyekaM prapaJNchAkAreNa brahma vibhrAmyanti, sAdR^ishyAchcha prapaJNchaikatAvabhAsaH anekAvagatadvitIyachandravat.h, svarUpApekShayA cha brahma jagatkAraNamityeke | 
tatrAvAntarabhedamavivakShitvA dvedhaiva vikalpitam.h | iha jIvagetyanuktvA tato.anyageti vadatA sa jIvaH kiM brahmaNo.anyo(.ananyo vA) na vA ityapi vikalpaH sUchitaH | tatra dvitIyaH prathame pravishatIti taM dUShayati- brahmaNashchediti ||
yadi brahmaNo vi(shva)bhramastadA bhramasya visheShAj~nAnapUrvakatvAttadapi brahmaNo.aN^gIkaraNIyam.h | tathAcha tasya sArvaj~nyaM na syAt.h | yadi cha na brahmaNi sArvaj~nyaM, tarhi kva tatsyAt.h | na tAvajjIve, anubhavavirodhAt.h | nApi jaDe, j~nAnamAtrAsambhavAt.h | tathAcha "yaH sarvaj~naH' ityAdishrutivaiyarthyaM syAt.h | nanu sArvaj~nyamapi brahmaNo bhrAntyaiveti chenna | yAdR^ishatAdR^ishasyApi visheShaj~nAnavirodhitvAt.h | anyathA shuktij~nAnavato.api tadaj~nAnaM na viruddhayateti bhramAnuchChedaprasaN^gaH | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | brahmaNo visheShAbhAvAttadanavabhAsanimitto bhramo nopapadyate | svarUpaM tu svaprakAshatayA siddham.h | asiddhatve vA(cha) sutarAM vibhramAnupapattiH | adhiShThAnAnupalambhAdityapi draShyavyam.h | 
dvitIyasyAdyaM dUShayati- anyagA chediti ||
yadi brahmavyatiriktajIvAshrayA vishvabhrAntiraN^gIkriyate tadA bhrAntyAshrayasya bhrAntikalpitatvAyogAt.h jIvabrahmaNoranyatA svAbhAvikItyApannam.h | tatashchApasiddhAnta iti | 
nanvastu jIvabrahmabhedo vAstavaH | anAtmaprapaJNcho.astu bhrAntikalpito brahmaNItyata Aha- neti ||
yadyapi naivaM mAyAvAdino manyante | tathA.api sUtrArthanirAkaraNAya pravR^ittasya tatraivAnupapattivyutpAdanaM shlAghyamityArambhaH | na kevalaM brahmavyatiriktAnAM jIvAnAmakalpitatvam.h | kintu dehayogarahitasyendriyAbhAvAtatpadArthadarshanaM na sambhavatItyato hetoH AropakAraNamindriyaM tadAshrayo dehashcha kalpanAM vinaivAstItyaN^gIkaraNIyam.h | nahi sukhAdivadrajatAdivadvA.asya prapaJNchasya sAkShimAtrasiddhatvaM paro manyate dehendriyANAmapyutpattimatvAt.h | tatkAraNaM cha svata ityaN^gIkaraNIyam.h | 
astu brahmavyatiriktAnAM jIvAnAM sakAraNAnAM tadIyadehendriyANAM chAbhrAntikalpitatvam.h | draShyR^itvena darshanakaraNatvena tadAshrayatvena tatkAraNatvena cha bhrAnteH pUrvabhAvitvAt.h | tadatiriktAstu prapaJNcho.astu bhrAntikalpita ityata Aha- dehina iti ||
kAraNashabdena j~nAnakAraNAnAmindriyANAM dehendriyakAraNAnAM cha grahaNam.h | siddhA iti sheShaH | kiM AkShepe | tatra tarhi prapaJNche brahmaNIti vA | anantajIvasakAraNadehendriyAtiriktasya prapaJNchasyAbhAvAt.h | viShayANAmapi dehendriyanirvAhArthatvAditi bhAvaH | tathAcha na kevalamapasiddhAntaH | prakR^itishchetyAdisUtrANAM nirviShayatvApattishcha syAditi sheShaH | 
nanu anyagA chetsvato.anyatA ityuktam.h | jIvabrahmabhedasyApi bhrAntisiddhatvAt.h | bhrAntyA brahmaNo bhinnasya bAhyAdhyAtmikArthabhrama iti hi manyata ityata Aha- bhedo.apIti || 
na kevalaM prapaJNchaH, kintu jIvabrahmaNorbhedo.api yadi bhramajo bhramasiddhaH aN^gIkriyate | tadA anyonyAshrayatA syAditi sambandhaH | 
atrAnyonyAshrayatAshabdena chakrakamuchyate tasyApi bahuShvanyonyAshrayatvAt.h | kathamanyonyAshrayatA ityata uktam.h- bhrAnteriti ||
bhrAntejarIvabrahmabhedahetorbhAvarUpAj~nAnakAraNatvAt.h | tasyAj~nAnasya cha bhedasApekShatvAt.h | aj~nAnamanAditvAtkathaM bhedavyapekShayA syAdityata uktam.h- nAj~nAneti ||
yato brahmavyatiriktajIvAdR^ite nAj~nAnakalpakaM kiJNchidasti |
etaduktaM bhavati | jIvabrahma(NoH)bhedo yayA bhrAntyA siddhaH, sA tAvadaj~nAnApekShA | bhrAnteH svarUpato viShayashchAj~nAnakAryatvAN^gIkArAt.h | yadyapi bhedaviShayA bhrAntiH sAkShichaitanyam.h | tathA.api tasyAsaN^gasyAropitArthasaMsR^iShyarUpaM(patA) nAj~nAnena vinotpadyate | tachchAj~nAnaM bhedasApekSham.h | anAditve.api bhrAntikalpitatvasyAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | anyathA satyatApAtAt.h | bhrAnteH (cha) jIvAshritatvasyAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | bhedakalpanayA vinA cha jIvasyAbhAvAt.h | na chAvidyAropo brahmaNyeveti yuktam.h | sarvasyApi tadAshrayatvopapattau ardhajaratIyAnupapatteH | ato bhramaj~nAnajIvabhedAnAmanyasApekShatvAchchakrakamiti |
athavA  bhedasya bhrAntikalpitatve bhrAnteshcha bhedasApekShatvAdanyonyAshrayatvamanenoktam.h | vyutpAdanArthamevAj~nAnaM madhye niveshitamiti draShyavyam.h | anena jIvAj~nAnavAdo(pakSho).api nirastaH | itaretarAshrayAdidoShasAmyAt.h | bIjAN^kuravadadoSha iti chenna | vaiShamyAt.h | vyaktibhedena hi tatrAdoShatvam.h | nacha jIvAvidyavyaktibhedo.astIti |
yaduktaM nAdehayogina ityAdi tadanupapannam.h | dehAderapi bhrAntikalpitatvAt.h | nacha tatra kAraNAbhAvaH pUrvadehAdervidyamAnatvAt.h | nachaivamanavasthA, anAditvAditi | maivam.h | Adisarge dehAdidarshanAnupapatteH | na hyayaM sAkShimAtrasiddho.artha ityuktam.h | kiJNcha syAdayamanavasthAparihAraH, yadi pUrvapUrvatarAdidehAderapi bhrAntisiddhatvaM pramitaM syAt.h | anyathaivaM, sarvatrAnavasthAparihAraH prasajyeta | nachAtra pramANaM asti | nanu kathaM nAsti, "neha nAnA' ityAdishrutervidyamAnatvAditi etadAha(ityata Aha)- bhramatve tviti ||
yadvA sarvo.apyayaM prasaN^go viparyayapayarvasAnahInatvAdAbhAsa eva | neha nAnetyAdishrutyA sarvasyApi viyadAdeH prapaJNchasya bhrAntikalpitatvAbhidhAnAt.h ityAshaN^kayedamuditam.h | upapattyaviruddho hi vedArtho grAhyaH | anyathA andho maNimavindat.h ityAderapi grahaNaprasaN^gAt.h | vichArashAstrAnArambhaprasaN^gAchcha | neha nAnetyAdivAkyaM chopapattiviruddham.h | tathAhi | yadi viyadAdikaM sarvaM bhramasiddhaM syAt.h tadA tadantaHpAtitvAdiyaM shrutishcha tathA syAt.h | bhramAropitaM viyadAdikaM sarvaM bhramasiddhaM syAt.h tadA tadantaHpAtitvAdiyaM shrutishcha tathA syAt.h | bhramAropitaM chAsaditi shruterapyasattvAnnArthadhIhetutvamiti | bhramashabdaH j~nAne arthe cha pareShAM prasiddha iti bhramatva ityuktam.h | yadyapyayamarthaH prathamasUtre varNitaH tathA.api tatrAdhyAtmikaH prasaN^gaH (prapaJNcho) atra tu bAhyaShavaShaya iti bhedaH | adhikavivakShayA choktasya punaruktiriti | 
nanu sarvo.apyayaM prapaJNcho bhrAntisiddho.api vyAvahAriko bhavatyeva | atastadantaHpatitA shrutirapi vyAvahArikatvAdarthaheturbhaviShyatItyata Aha- vyAvahArikateti ||
chastvarthaH | syAdapyevaM yadi prapaJNchasya vyAvahArikatA tAvat.h (tava) shakyAN^gIkArA syAt.h | na chaivam.h | yato.asya prapaJNchasya vyAvahArikatA tu abAdhyatva eva syAt.h | etaduktaM bhavati | yadi prapaJNcho vyAvahAriko.aN^gIkriyeta, tarhyabAdhyo.apyaN^gIkartavyaH prasajyeta | nacha tathA.aN^gIkriyate bhavatA | ato na vyAvahArikA.apyaN^gIkartumuchita iti | satyatvAN^gIkArApAdane tviShyApAdanaM syAt.h | pareNApi kathaJNchitsatyatvasyApyaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | ato.abAdhyatva evetyuktam.h | 
nanu shaktirajatAderbAdhyasyApyabhij~nAbhivadanarUpavyavahAraviShayatvAdvayAptihIno.ayaM tarka ityata Aha- bAdhyamiti ||
satyaM bAdhyaM shuktirajatAdikam.h, abhij~nAdikaM vyavahAraviShaya iti | tathApyarthakriyAkAri na bhavati | nahi tena rajatochitA valayanirmANAdyarthakriyAjAyamAnA dR^iShyA | arthakriyAkAritvalakShaNameva vyAvahArikatvamiha prakR^itam.h | nAbhij~nAdiviShayatvam.h | shruterarthadhIjanakatvopanyastatvAt.h | ato na tarkasyAN^gavaikalyamiti |
nanu bAdhyatvaM shuktikAdyadhiShThAnasya dharmaH | "vij~nAtasyAnyathA' ityuktatvAt.h | shuktikAdikaM chArthakriyAkArIti kathamuchyate bAdhyaM nArthakriyAkArIti | maivam.h | niShedhyatvalakShaNabAdhyatvasya parAbhyupagatasyAtrAshrayaNAt.h | 
nanu tathA.apyasatyasya svApnakAminIsambhogAdeH charamadhAtuvisargAdyarthakriyAkAritvadarshanAt.h vyAptivikalastarka ityata Aha- na cheti || 
svapna iti svapnAvasthopalabdho.arthaH | no.asmAkaM bAdarAyaNIyAnAM mate | tarhi mama matena vyAptibhaN^go.astu mayA mR^iShAtvenAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h iti chenna, bAdarAyaNIyena tathA.aN^gIkartumashakyatvAt.h | nanu kathaM bAdarAyaNasya na mR^iShA svapna ityata Aha- vAsaneti ||
tasya svapnasyApi mAyAmAtramiti vadatA sUtrakAreNa vAsanAjanitatvenAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h idaM j~nAyate, yat.h na tasya svapno mR^iShA.abhimata iti | nahi kashchidavidyamAnasya kAraNaM nirUpayet.h | kiJNcha shrutyanusArI hi sUtrakArasya siddhAntaH syAt.h | shrutyA cha svApnArthasya kartAraM vadantyA satyatvamevAbhipretamiti na mR^iShAtvaM sUtrakR^ito.abhimatamityAha- sa hIti ||
nanu kathaM svapno na mR^iShA | "mAyAmAtram.h' iti sUtrakR^itaiva tanmithyAtvasya vakShyamANatvAdityato vAha- vAsaneti ||
na mAyAmAtrapadena svapnasya mR^iShAtvamabhimatam.h, kintu vAsanAjanitatvam.h, ato na mR^iShetyarthaH | yathA chaitattathA upapAdayiShyate | tasyAgAminaH sUtrasya vAsanAjanitatvapratipAdakatvena asmAbhiraN^gIkR^itatvAditi vA yojyam.h | na kevalaM vakShyamANopapattivashAt.h mR^iShAtvaM na sUtrArthaH | kintu shrutivashAchchetyAha- sa hIti ||
yadvA svApnArtho na tAvadanAdinityaH, pashchAt.h adR^iShyayAdivirodhAt.h | nApi sAdivinAshI, upAdAnanimittayoranirUpaNAt.h | nacha prakArAntaraM sambhavati | tatkathaM na mR^iShetyata Aha- vAsaneti || nopAdAnAbhAva iti sheShaH | "na mR^iShA' iti pUrveNa vA sambandhaH | evam.h upAdAnaM nirUpya nimittamupapAdayati- sahIti || nimittaM cheshvaro j~nAyate, iti sheShaH | "na mR^iShA' iti pUrveNaiva vA anvayaH | 
nanu kathaM tarhi "svapnamAyAsarUpA' ityAdau svapnasya bhrAntitvoktirityata Aha- jAgratvamiti ||
itishabda Adyarthe, ullekhAthare vA | jAgradahamasmIti draShyuryajjAgrattvaM, yachchaitatpadArthAnAM jAgra(d.hdR^ishA dR^ishAdR^iShyapadArthaiH aikyaM, bAhyamR^idAdijanyatvaM vA, evamAdipratibhAso bhramaH | bAdhyatvAditi hishabdArthaH | tadapekShayA shrutyAdivachanAnIti bhAvaH | 
nanu cha rajjau sarpabhrame, asatyasyApi sarpasya sarpochitabhayakampAdyarthakriyAkAritvaM dR^ishyate, tathA sarpe samAropitAyAH kusumamAlAyAH santoShakAritA upalabhyate, ato vyAptibhaN^gastarkasyetyata Aha- sarpeti ||
"nA bhUdatra sarpaH' itivat.h "na sarpaj~nAnamabhUt.h' iti bAdhakAnudayAt.h | abhUdevetyanuvR^itteshcha | bhramatvasya viShayavaiparItyamAtreNopapatteriti hishabdArthaH | ki(mato)ntato yadi j~nAnamastyevetyata Aha- tadeveti ||
evashabdena sarpAdikaM vyAvataryati | satyapi sarpAdau asati cha j~nAne, bhayakampAdyanutpatteH | sati cha (tasmin.h) tadutpatterj~nAnakAryameva bhayakampAdikaM na sarpakAryam.h | tatkAryaM tu abhisarpaNadaMshanAdikam.h | maraNamapi dhAtuvyAkulatAnimittakam.h | sA cha viShadravyeNeva bhayAdinA.api bhavatIti na bAdhyasya(syApi) sarpAderarthakriyAkAritvam.h | 
nanu kiM j~nAnamAtraM bhayAdijanakaM kiMvA viShayAvachChinnam.h | nAdyaH | ghaTaj~nAnasyApi j~nAnatvena tadApatteH | dvitIye na tAvadviShayo rajjvAdiH | rajjuriyamityAdi j~nAnasyApi bhayAdihetutApAtAt.h | sarpAdishchedvisheShaNatayA tasyApi bhayAdihetutvaM prAptam.h | 
atra kashchidAha | nAyaM doShaH, j~nAnavyAvartakatayopayuktasya sarpAderviShayasya j~nAnajanyArthakriyAyAmapraveshAt.h | nahi kurUNAM kShetre vasati, gurUNAM TIkAM paThati ityAdau visheShaNasyApi kArakatvamasti | kintvatiprasaktayoH kShetraTIkayorvyAvR^ittimAtreNa charitArthatvamiti | tadasat.h | evamapi bAdhyasya sarpAdervyAvartakatvasyAvashyAbhyupagamanIyatvAt.h | vyAvR^ittibuddhijanakatvaM hi vyAvartakatvam.h | tatrApi j~nAnAbhyupagamena parihAre vyAvartakopAdAnena prasaN^gatAdavasthyamiti | tatrAha- tAdR^ishamiti || yAdR^ishaM satyasarpollekhi j~nAnaM, tAdR^ishamityarthaH |
satyasarpaj~nAnaM tAvadghaTAdij~nAnAdvayAvR^ittamanubhUyate | vyAvR^ittishcha vyAvartaka(dharma)yogakR^itA sarvatropalabdhA | nacha viShayo vyAvartakaH, tasyAtaddharmatvAt.h | sambaddhaM hi vyAvartakaM bhavati | anyathA.atiprasaN^gAt.h | viShayasambandho vyAvartako.astviti chenna | tasya saMyogAdirUpasyAbhAvAt.h | ataH kashchijj~nAnagata eva dharmo.abhyupagantavyaH | 
kiJNcha vilakShaNasamAgrIjanmanorj~nAnayoryathA parokShatvAparokShatvarUpo visheShaH viShayopAdhinA vinA.abhyupagamyate, evamaparokShaj~nAne.api kathaM svagato visheSho nAN^gIkaraNIyaH | api cha sarpaj~nAnasya vilakShaNArthakriyA na svagatenAtishayena vinopapadyate | nahi 
devadattasambandhitAmAtreNa kalamabIjaM kalamabIjAntarakAryavilakShaNaM kAryamupajanayati | sa chAyaM visheShaH satyasarpaj~nAne samIchInayA sAmagyrA jAtaH, mithyAsarpaj~nAne tvasamIchInayA iti na kashchidvisheShaH | ato viShayAntarbhAvamantareNa svagatenaiva visheSheNa sarpAdij~nAnasya bhayAdijanakatvAnna sarpasya kiJNchitkaratvamiti | tadevaM yatrAtharkriyA nishchitA na tatra mithyAtvam.h, yatra tu mithyAtvaM na tatrArthakriyeti na tarkamUlavyApteH kvApi bhaN^gaH, ityupasaMharati- taditi ||   Vyasa-(5) 
nanvarthakriyAkAritvaM yathA vipakShAnmithyAbhUtAdvayAvR^ittam.h evaM sapakShAdbrahmaNo.api vyAvR^ittatvAdasAdhAraNam.h | nacha j~nAnasya satyasyArthakriyokteti vAchyam.h, tasyApi prapaJNchAntarbhAvena vipratipannatvAdityata Aha- brahma tviti ||
tena mAyAvAdinaiva brahma prapaJNchAdapyatishayenArthakriyAkAryamaN^gIkR^itameva hi janmAdisUtre jagatkAraNatvenoktatvAt.h | ataH sapakShapraveshitvAnnAsAdhAraNyaM mantavyam.h | nanu mayA.aN^gIkriyamANaM brahmaNo.arthakriyAkAritvaM cha na svAbhAvikam.h | kintu parata eva | mAyAyAM tadApa(yattami)tata ityaN^gIkArAt.h | ataH kathamApAdakasya sapakShapravesha ityata Aha- parata iti ||
aN^gIkR^itaM tAvadarthakriyAkAritvaM brahmaNaH, tatsvataH parato vA.astu kimanena prakR^itAnupayuktena | nahi svato.arthakriyAkAritvamApAdakatvenAsmAbhirabhihitam.h, pareNa vA prastAvitam.h | anyathA sAmAnyataH prayuktasya dhUmAdervisheShAkAreNa sapakShApraveshitayA.asAdhAraNya(Na)sya vaktuM shakyatvena tadbhaN^gaH syAt.h | 
ayamatrAshayaH | brahmaNo jagannirmANAdyarthakriyA pratItA na vA | na chetkathaM lakShaNatvenochyate | kasya cha mAyAmayatvamaN^gIkriyate | pratItatve.api na tAvatpratyakShAnumAnAbhyAm.h | tadagocharatvAt.h | ataH shrutyaiveti vaktavyam.h | tathAcha kathaM mAyikatvam.h | tatkiM shrutipratItaM sarvameva satyam.h | addhA | bAdhakAbhAve tu tathaiva | nachaivaM brahmaNo.arthakriyAyAH paratastve pramANamasti yadbAdhakaM bhavet.h | bAdhakAbhAvamAtreNa kathaM satyArthatvamiti chet.h | prAmANyasya svatastvAditi brUmaH | paratastve cha prAmANyasyAnavasthApAtena na pramA nishchIyeta | santi "niShphalaM niShkriyam.h' ityAdishrutayo bAdhikA iti chet.h | evaM shrutibalena parastve.arthakriyAyAH svIkR^ite tadabhidhAtrI "sa idaM sarvamasR^ijata' ityAdishrutirna pramA syAt.h | pratipAditArthamithyAtvAtiriktasyAprAmANyasyAbhAvAt.h | kiJNchAvisheShAt.h "niShkalaM niShkriyam.h' iti shrutiretachChativirodhAtparatastve na prameti kiM na syAt.h | anyaduttaratra vakShyAma iti |
nanvastvabAdhyamevArthakriyAkAri prapaJNchamapyabAdhyamaN^gIkaromi | AtyantikAbAdhyatvAbhAve.api prAgbrahmAtmaikyaj~nAnAdabAdhyatvAt.h | atastadantargatA shrutirapyamukhyasatyatvAtsAdhikA bhaviShyatItyata Aha- amukhyeti ||
sadA itya(nena)sya prameyasya prAgevopapAditatvamityAchaShye | tatashcha punaruktidoShaH parihR^ito bhavati | tiShThatu na vaktavyeti yAvat.h | sA pramA brahmaj~nAnabAdhyaM pramANamityarthaH | yasmAtsA shrutirapramA tasmAttiShThatviti vA | prapaJNchamithyAtvaM hi tadatharH | na chAsau brahmasvarUpam.h | sopAdhikatvAt.h | tato.asya bAdhyatvamAvashyakam.h | bAdhyArthaM chApramANamiti prasiddhameva | bAdhyArthatve.api prAgbrahmaj~nAnAdabAdhyArthatvena prAmANyamastvityata uktam.h- amukhyeti || satyamabAdhyArtham.h | nahi kAlavilambena bAdhitArthaM pramANaM bhavatIti vakShyAmaH | astvevaM svarUpato viShayatashchAsatyatvAtsAdhakatvena vipratipannA shrutiH, tathA.api prapaJNchamithyAtvasAdhanAya tadupanyAsaH kuto na kAryaH ityata Aha- na hIti ||
tathAtve svarUpAsiddhakAlAtItayorapyupanyAsaH syAt.h | AropamAtrasya tatrA.api sulabhatvAditi bhAvaH | 
syAdetat.h | AstAmiyaM pramANasadasattvachintA | pramANenaiva prameyasiddheH | anyathA bhavatAmapi prapaJNchamithyAtvanirAkaraNe tatsatyatvasAdhane cha pramANAbhAvena kathA.abhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | yuShmAbhirupanyasyamAnaM pramANaM satyamasatyaM vA syAt.h | na tAvatsatyaM mAM prati vaktumuchitam.h mayA satyasya sAdhakatvAnaN^gIkArAt.h, yatsatyaM na tatra kriyA.a.aveshaH yatra cha kriyA.a.avesho na tatsatyamiti | nacha vAchyaM sAkShiNaH satyasya sAdhakatvaM tvayAN^gIkR^itamiti | kathachchitsukhAdau tasya shakyopanyAsatve.api bAhyaprapaJNche tadayogAt.h | bAhyapramANaviShayo hyasau | anyathA.andhabadhirAdyabhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | sa eva chAtra prakR^ita iti | nApyasatyaM bhavadbhiranaN^gIkR^itatvAdityata Aha- sAdhakatvamiti ||
satyasya tviti sambandhaH | samyagiti mukhyata eva, na tvadhikaraNasiddhAntatvena | hishabdaH, sarvaM vastu j~nAtatayA.aj~nAtatayA vA sAkShichaitanyasya viShaya evetyAditatprasiddhidyotakaH | tadityavyayam.h | tena sAkShiNA | vishvavivartamataM na bhavet.h | nirAkurma iti yAvat.h | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | vishvasya satyatAmapi tenaiva sAdhayAma ityapi draShyavyam.h | tathAcha vakShyate | 
na kApi pramANaprameyAdivyavasthA mayAN^gIkR^itA | kintu parakIyarItyaiva sarvamuchyate | tatkathaM kimapyanaN^gIkurvANaM mAM prati sAkShiNaH sAdhakatvaM tvayA.aN^gIkR^itamityuchyata ityata Aha- yadIti ||
na vidyate.aN^gIkR^itamaN^gIkAro yasyetyanaN^gIkR^itaH | tasya bhAvo.anaN^gIkR^itatA | anaN^gIkAritvamityarthaH | itishabdadvayaM hetau | yadi paro brUyAnmayA kiJNchinnAN^gIkR^itamiti | tadA.asau vaktavyaH | sarvathA.anaN^gIkR^itatvam.h AtmanastvayA.aN^gIkR^itaM na vA | Adye(.api) kiJNchidapi nAN^gIkR^itamiti pakShahAneH Atmano.anaN^gIkartR^itApi nAN^gIkR^iteti dvitIya evAN^gIkaraNIyaH | tathAcha asau mUkaH syAt.h | aN^gIkArAnaN^gIkArodAsInasya mR^itakasyeva vAkyapravR^itterayuktatvAt.h | tathAcha maunamavalambamAnasya nAsmatprativAditeti kimatra vaktavyam.h | satyametat.h | vastutastu vayaM sarvato nivR^ittAH svataH siddhe chidAtmani brahmatatve kevale bhAramavalambya charitArthAH sukhamAsmahe | ye tu svaparikalpitasAdhanadUShaNAdivyavasthayA vichAramavatArya tattvaM nirNetumichChanti tAnprati brUmo na sAdhvIyaM bhavatAM vichAravyavastheti | maivam.h | evamapi parakIyavichAravyavasthiterasAdhutvasyAvashyamaN^gIkaraNIyatvAt.h | anyathA tad.hvyutpAdanaM vyarthaM syAt.h | 
ata tanmAtramaN^gIkR^itya pramANAdivyavasthA nAN^gIkR^iteti manyase | tanna | pramANAdinA vinA paravyavasthAyA asAdhutvasya vyutpAdayitumashakyatvAt.h | bhavatkalpitavyavasthaiva vyAhatatvAdasAdhvI bhavadvayavastheti brUmo na punaratra kimapi pramANamaN^gIkurma iti chenna, yatsvAbhyupagatavyavasthAviruddhaM tadasAdhvityasyApi pramANasyAN^gIkartavyatvAt.h | etadapi pareNAbhyupagatamevAshrIyata iti chet.h na | kiM parakIyavyavasthAyA asAdhutvasvayamavabuddhaya paraM prati bodhyate.anavabuddhayaiva vA | dvitIye vipralambhakatvaM syAt.h | vijigIShukathAyAmevameveta chet.h na | shiShyasyApi boddhayatvAt.h | Adye.asmAdanyasmAdvA pramANAtsvayaM boddhavyam.h | tatkathaM pramANAdyanaN^gIkatarR^itvam.h | pramitikaraNatvAdinopAdAnasyaiva pramANAdyaN^gIkAritvAt.h | tasmAt.h sattvAsattvA(satyatvAsatyatvA)bhyupagamodAsInaiH pramANAdikamaN^gIkR^ityochyata iti vaktavyam.h | tachcha prAgeva nirastamiti |
evaM vishvasya brahmavivartatvaM nirAkR^itya tatsa(ttA)tyatAyAM pramANamAha- vishvamiti || 
yathArthata ityanena "kavirmanIShI' iti shrutimupAdatte | vyAvahArikasatyatAparAH shrutaya iti chenna | "tatsatyam.h' ityasyA api tathAtvaprasaN^gAt.h | shrutyantaravirodhAditi chedatrApi "asadevedam.h' iti shrutivirodhAt.h | apuruShArthatvAnna prapaJNchasatyatAyAM tAtparyamiti chenna | satyajagannirmAtR^itvAdipArameshvaramAhAtmyaj~nAnasyaiva puruShArthahetu(prayojana)tvAt.h | niShprapaJNchAtmaj~nAnasAdhyAdvitIyatApattirupapuruShArthaviruddhaM prapaJNchasatyatvamiti chet.h tarhi brahmasatyatvamapi shUnyaparibhAvanAlabhyashUnyatApattilakShaNamokShaviruddhamiti samAnam.h | tat.h pramANAnanuguNamiti chet.h | samametadapIti vakShyAmaH | anumAnamapi prapaJNchasatyatAyAmatharkriyAkAritvaM draShyavyam.h | prAguktatarkopapAdanenaiva asyopapAditvAditi | 
evamAgamAnumAnAbhyAM siddhe vishvasatyatve pratyakShamapyAha- satyatvamiti ||
chashabdaH pramANasamuchchaye | na kevalamAntarasya sukhAdeH kintu bAhyasya gaganAdeshcheti vA | tatrApi kAlagaganadigAdayaH sAkShAtsAkShisiddhasatyatvAH | stambhakumbhAdayastu vakShyamANena prakAreNeti j~nApayituM gaganAderityuktam.h | anyathA vishvasya prakR^itatvAttadevAtrAnuvartiShyate kimanena | sAkShItyevokte sAkShiNo.aprAmANyAt.h prAmANye vA pramANatritvabhaN^gAt.h na vishvasatyatvaM pramitamiti shaN^kA syAt.h | tannivR^ittyarthaM pratyakShetyuktam.h | tathAcha vakShyate | pratyakShetyevokte atIndriyArthasatyatAyAM na pramANamuktaM syAt.h | nacha sAkShirA vinA bAhyapratyakShamAtreNaindriyakANAmapi satyatA siddhayatItyataH sAkShItyuktam.h | ubhayavAdisiddhaM pramANamasmatpakShe.astItyuktenaiva asyArthasya labdhatvAtsAdhitamityAha | tathA.api tadupapAdanAya punurupanyAsaH |

nanu viShama upanyAsaH | bhUtalAbhAvayorasti sAnnidhyam.h | tena sambandhAbhAve.api bhaviShyati vishiShyavyavahAraH | darshanasya durapahnavatvAt.h | sambandhAntarakalpanasya cha vyarthatvAt.h | nacha taraNiparispandAnAM piNDasAnnidhyamasti | tato bhavitavyaM madhye dravyAntareNeti | maivam.h | vinA.api sAnnidhyena ghaTaj~nAnamiti vishiShyapratyayadarshanAt.h  | 
kiJNchAbhAvasyApi na bhUtalasAnnidhyaM parapakShe kimapi pashyAmaH | astu vA tapanaparispandAnAM piNDaM pratyupanAyakaM dravyAntaram.h | tachcha pR^ithivyAdikaM kiM na syAt.h | tapanapiNDAbhyAmasaMsargAnneti chenna | ekaikasyAvyApakatve.api bahUnAM saMyuktasaMyogabhUyastvena kriyopanAyakatvopapatteH | nacha taraNipiNDAntakAle tAni na santyanupalambhAditi vAchyam.h | sUkShmANAM kalpanIyatvAt.h | nacha vinigamanAyAM kAraNAbhAvaH | saMshaye.api parisheShAvadhAraNAnupapatteH | dharmikalpanAto dharmakalpanasya laghIyastvAt.h | AkAsho vA kiM na syAt.h | na syAt.h | visheShaguNavattvAtpR^ithivyAdivaditi chenna | visheShaNaguNavato.api nIladravyasya paTe nIlimopasaN^krAmakatvadarshanAt.h | sUryagatyupanAyakatvaM cha dravyasvarUpaM vA atIndriyashaktirvA sahakArishaktirvA | nAdyaH | dravyamAtre prasaN^gAt.h | na dvitIyaH | anabhyupagamAt.h | tR^itIye(.api) kiM tadvayApakatvaM vA, visheShaguNaviraho veti va(vive)ktavyam.h |   Vyasa-(6) 
yaM tu brUmaH | vyApakatvameva taditi | anyathA manaso.api tatprasaN^gAt.h | vyApakatvasya prayojakatAyAmAtmano.api tatprasaN^ga iti chenna | tadvayApakatvAbhAvasya vakShyamANatvAt.h | vyApakatve.apyaniShyAbhAvAt.h | kriyopanAyakatvaM khalvAntarAlikasya dravyasya nobhayasaMyogAtiriktaM kiJNchit.h | tadekasyevAnekeShAmapi samAnam.h | yadyAkAshaM(H) svasambandhenAnyagataM dharmam.h anyatra saN^krAmayet.h, tadA sarvaM sarvatra saN^krAmayet.h avisheShAditi chenna | niyatopasaN^krAmakatvasyaiva kalpanIyatvAt.h | gurvI hi dharmamAtrakalpanAto dharmikalpanA | anyathA kAle.api samAnaH prasaN^gaH | tatsiddhayasiddhibhyAmanavasaraduHsthatvamiti chenna | bhAvAnavabodhAt.h | vishiShyapratyayadarshanAnantaraM bahavaH pakShAH prApnuvanti | kimayaM svarasambandhanibandhanaH kiM vA atiriktasambandhAdhIna iti | dvitIye.api kiM sAkShAtsambandho.atra nimittamuta dravyAntarakR^ita iti | uttaratrApa taddravyaM prasiddheShvanyatamaM vA bhavatvanyadveti | sarvatra bAdhakAni paryAlochayanprasiddhadravyeShu yadbAdhakaM pashyettadaprasiddhe.api kalpyamAne kathaM nAnusandadhyAt.h | anusandadhAnashcha tatsvAbhAvyena parihAraM chintayankalpanAgauravavyasanamapahAya laghIyAMsameva pakShaM na kathaM(vA) rochayata ityasyArthasya vivakShitatvAt.h | para(pra)siddhatvena prasaN^gasya na doSha ityasyApyayamevAbhiprAyaH | 
kiJNchAyaM prasaN^go vastutaH sAdhuH athAbhAsaH | nAdyaH | kAlapratItyuttarakAlaM vyAptibhaN^gAt.h | dvitIye kathamAkAshasya kriyopanAyakatvaM tyAjayet.h | anyathA jAtinirAkaraNamapi na syAditi | 
astu vA.a.akAshasya visheShaguNavataH kriyopanAyakatvAbhAvaH dishastu syAt.h visheShaguNashUnyatvAt.h vyApakatvAchcha | tasyAH saMyogopanAyakatvena siddhatvAnneti chenna | ubhayopanAyakatve.api bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | sahakAribhedena cha vyavasthitAvyavasthitapratItijanakatvaM kalpyatAM lAghavAdeva | anyathA kAle.api bhedakalpanAprasaN^gAditi | tadidamuktam.h | tasya vishiShyapratyayasya nityena niyatena prasiddhenaiva pR^ithivyAdinA siddhernAprasiddhe dravye.anumAnAvasaro bhavediti |
anye tu paramparashabdAbhyAM paratvAparatve guNau yuvasthavirapiNDa(vartinau)gatau AchakShate | tau asamavAyikAraNasaMyogAshrayatayA nimittakAraNApekShAbuddhisampAdakatayA vA kAlamanumApayata iti | tadapyuktanyAyena nirastamiti |
kiJNcha parAparAdipratyayAnAM sUryagatayo vA parA(tvA)paratve vA yadyAlambanaM tadA astu kAlAnumAnam.h | na chaitadasti | kAlabhedAnAmeva visheShaNatayA pratIteH | tathAhi | paro.ayamityAdi prayuktavantaH ko.asyArtha iti pR^iShyAH laukikAH parIkShikAshcha bahukAlIna(no.ayamityAdi) iti vyAchakShANA dR^ishyante | tatra kAlasvarUpaM sAkShisiddham.h | tadbahutvAdi cha kvachitsAkShiNA kvachidanumAnAdinA cha j~nAyata iti | etadapyuktam.h tadetaditi shlokAbhyAm.h | anayaiva dishA disho.api parAparapratyayAdiliN^gatvaM nirAkartavyam.h | 
ta(me)detaM chirantanaM panthAnamarochayamAnA navInAstu dikkAlayoranyathAnumAnamAhuH | vivAdAdhyAsitaM kAryaM visheShaguNarahitadravyAbhyAM janyate kAryatvAt.h antaHkaraNadvayasaMyogavaditi |
(e)tada(pya)yuktam.h | sAdhye bahuvachanaprayoge(kShepe).atiprasaN^gAt.h | nacha dR^iShyAntAbhAvaH | antaHkaraNagatabahutvasya sattvAt.h | na chAntaHkaraNadvayasaMyoge pramANamasti, mano manasA saMyujyate mUrtatvAchCharIravaditi cha AkAlike vidyadAdau sandigdhavyabhichAram.h | 
apara Aha | paramamahatparimANaM dravyachatuShyayavR^itti parimANatvAdaNutvavaditi | atra yadyAkAshAtma(gata)parimANapakShIkArastadA siddhasAdhanam.h AtmanAM bahutvAt.h | AtmatvenaikyamupAdAya prayoge.api bAdhaH | parimANadvayasya dravyachatuShyayavR^ittitvAyogAt.h | ekaikadravyavR^itti khalu parimANam.h | ata eva na kAlAdigatasya pakShIkAraH | AshrayAsiddhishchAdhikA | 
paramamahatparimANasAmAnyaM visheShaguNashUnyadravyAdhikaraNAnekavyaktivR^itti parimANatAratamyavishrAntiviShayajAtitvAt.h aNuparimANavR^ittijAtivat.h iti chAnupapannam.h | paramamahatparimANasAmAnyaM hi parimANatvaM vA tadavAntarajAtirvA | Adye manaHsiddhayA.apyasya sambhavenArthAntaratA | sAmAnyasyApyanekavR^ittitAyA nirAkariShyamANatvena bAdhAshrayAsiddhI cha | na dvitIyaH | tasyAH (tasya) nirAkariShyamANatvAt.h | varNasiddhayA arthAntaratvAchcha | anekapadasthAne bahupadaprakShepe atiprasaN^gAchcha | 
astu kAlasya dishashcha bahutvam.h, AtmavadupasaN^grAhakaikyena dravyANAM navatvopapattiriti chettarhi dishA kAlena vA sAdhyaparyavasAnA(sambhavA)dubhayasAdhakatvamasya na syAt.h | mA bhUditi chenna | anekapadavaiyarthyAt.h | anyatarasAdhane.anyatareNArthAntaratAprasaN^gAt.h | hetudR^iShyAntayoshchAnupapattirvakShyata ityalaM pallavena |
gaganAdessakalaprapaJNchasya traikAlikAbAdhyatvaM sAkShisiddhamityuktamarthamupasaMharanvivR^iNoti- ata iti ||
na vidyate doShaH kAraNaM yasya j~nAnasya tena pratItasya viShayIkR^itasyAdoSheNa pratyakShAdinA vA pratItasya gaganAdeH prapaJNchasya satyatvaM traikAlikAbAdhyatvaM sAkShiNA mataM siddham.h | prAmANyagrahaNAdineti sheShaH | 
ayama(trA)bhiprAyaH | AkAshakAladigAtmamanAMsi sukhAdayashcha sAkShAtsAkShisiddhAH | taditare tu padArthA yathAsvam.h(yathAyatham.h) indriyaliN^gashabdagamyAH | j~nAnaM cha bhAvAbhAvalakShaNaM svaviShayaM sattvenaivAvagAhate, nAsattvena, nApyudAsInena rUpeNa | nachaivaM ghaTo.asti ghaTo nAstItipratyayAnupapattiH paunaruktyAdvayAghAtAchcheti yuktam.h | ghaTo.astIti deshakAlavisheShasambandhisattAviShayatvAt.h, kvachidviparItAkAN^kShAvyavachChedAthartvAt.h, kvApi vyAkhyAnavyAkhyeyabhAvAt.h | nAstItyasya cha deshakAlavisheShasambandhisattApratiShedhaparatvAt.h | nahi satA sakaladeshakAlasatA bhavitavyamiti niyAmakamasti | j~nAnagataM cha yAthArthyalakShaNaM prAmANyaM j~nAnagrAhakeNaiva gR^ihyate | j~nAnagrAhakashcha sAkShItyavivAdaM vAdiprativAdinoH | tathAcha sAkShiNA j~nAnaprAmANyaM gR^ihNatA tadviShayasya sakalaprapaJNchasya traikAlikAbAdhyatvalakShaNaM satyatvameva gR^ihItaM bhavati | yadi hi j~nAnagocharasya nityasya vA anityasya vA sarvagatasya vA asarvagatasya vA arthasya svadeshakAlaprakAropAdhAvasattvA.a.avedanalakShaNo bAdhaH syAt.h, ko.arthastadA j~nAnaprAmANyaM sAkShiNA pramitamityasyeti |
yadi tarhi j~nAnasvarUpagrAhakaH sAkShI tatprAmANyamapi gR^ihNanprapaJNchasatyatAM nishchinuyAt.h, shuktirajatAdij~nAnasvarUpagrAhako.api sa eveti tatprAmANyamapi gR^ihNan.h shuktirajatAdikamapi satyaM vyavasthApayet.h | nacha shuktirajatAdij~nAnAnAM prAmANyameva nAsti, kiM sAkShiNA gR^ihyatAm.h iti yuktam.h, prapaJNchagocharANAmapi j~nAnAnAM prAmANyAbhAvAtkiM sAkShirA gR^ihyata ityapi vaktuM shakyatvAt.h | tasmAtsAkShiNA prapaJNchasatyatAsiddhimabhilaShatA j~nAnagrAhakasya sAkShiNaH prAmANyagrAhakatvaM svabhAva iti vaktavyam.h | tathA chokto.atiprasaN^ga ityata uktam.h- adoSheti ||
ayamarthaH | na sAkShI j~nAnaM gR^ihNanpramANamevaitaditi gR^ihNAti | kintarhya(tva)doShaM chetpramANaM sadoShamapramANamiti vyavasthayA | yadA tvarthitvena prAmANyaM nirdidhArayiShitaM tadA sajAtIyavijAtIyasaMvAdavisaMvAdabhAvAbhAvalakShaNayA parIkShayA doShabhAvaM nishchitya 
prAmANyamavadhArayati doShadasharne tvaprAmANyam.h | prapaJNchapratIteshcha prayatnenAnviShyApi doShamapashyanprAmANyamevAvadhArayatIvati tatsatyatvaM sAkShisiddham.h | nachaivam.h shuktirajatAdInAm.h | doShApratItidashAyAM prAmANyAnavadhAraNAt.h, tatpratItau tvaprAmANyanishchayAt.h | nanu shuktirajatAdij~nAnasyApi prAmANyaM nirdhAryata eva | kathamanyathA niHshaN^kA pravR^ittiriti chet.h | satyam.h | nAsau sAkShirUpAvadhAraNA | api tu mAnasIti vakShyAmaH | manasashcha doShasaMsargasambhavena na tAvatA prAmANyasiddhiriti | 
nanu yadi parIkShAsahakR^itassAkShI j~nAnaprAmANyaM gR^ihNIyAt.h tadA.anavasthA syAt.h | parIkShA.api hi svayaM pramANatvenAvadhR^itA paraprAmANyAvadhAraNAyAlam.h | nAnyathA | tathAcha tatrApi parIkShAntaramavataraNIyamiti | kiJNcha sAkShiNo.apyanavadhR^itapramANabhAvasya svayaM duHsthasya na paraprAmANyAvadhAraNasamArthyamiti tatprAmANyAvadhAraNAya parIkShAntarApekShA grAhakAntarApekShA chetyanavasthaivetyata Aha- parIkShAdeshcheti ||
Adipadena sAkShI gR^ihyate | chastvarthaH | satyatvaM yathArthatvam.h | tena sAkShiNaiva kevalena na tu parIkShAyuktena(sahakR^itena) | hishabdo.asyArthasyAnubhavasiddhatvaM dyotayati | tasmAnnAnavastheti hetau vA | 
etaduktaM bhavati | doShAbhAvAvadhAraNArthaM nyAyAnusandhAnaM hi khalu parIkShA | sandigdhashchArtho nyAyaviShayaH | sandehashchobhayakoTiprApakasadbhAve bhavati | evaJNcha yatra yatra doShasambhAvanayA tatsandehastatra tatraiva parIkShApekShA nAnyatra | nacha sarvatra doShasandeho.asti | sAkShisiddhe.arthe tatprAptyabhAvAt.h | ato na tAvatparIkShA.anavasthA | tathAhi | astyatra purataH pAnIyamiti vAkyaM shrutavato bhavati sandehaH kimidaM viparyayAdimUlamuta neti | puruShavachasAmubhayathA darshanAt.h | tata evArthe sandihAnaH pratyAsIdan.h rUpavisheShAdinA.anuminoti pAnIyametaditi | tatrApi bhavati saMshayaH | kimidamanumAnamutAbhAsam.h(sa) iti | vyAptyAdigrAhiNAM yAthArthyAyAthArthyopalambhAt.h | pratyAsannashchodakAbhyavahArAnantaraM rasavisheShANAnumAyApi pUrvavatsandigdhe | pItodakastUdanyAdinimittaduHkhAbhAvaM sukhaM chAnubhavanna tatra saMshete | sukhAdau tadabhAve cha sAkShisiddhe kadA.apyanyathAbhAvAdyanupalambhAt.h | nacha pratItatvasAmAnyena tatrApi saMshayaH | visheShaniShThasya nishchAyakasya sadbhAvAt.h | anyathA saMshayAnuchChedena vyavahArAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | saMshayAbhAve cha na tatpUrvikA parIkSheti kuto.anavasthA | ata eva sAkShaprAmANyAvadhAraNe parIkShA.anavasthA.api parihR^itA | grAhakAnavasthA tu nAstyeva | sAkShiNaH svaprakAshatvena svaprAmANyagrAhakatvAt.h | 
etAvAnatra visheShaH | indriyaliN^gashabdajanyeShu j~nAneShvanAdau saMsAre dvayIM gatimanusandadhatsAkShI na sahasaiva pramANametaditi nishchetuM shaknoti | kintu dAShAbhAvanishchayadvAraiva | doShAbhAvaM cha na svayam.h(eva) avadhArayitumIShye | (api) kiM tu parIkShAsahakR^ita eva | parIkShAyAM chendriyaliN^gashabdajAyAM pUrvanyAyena parIkShAntaramanusarati yAvatsAkShAtsvaviShaye sukhAdAvavatarati | nacha svAtmanyanena kadA.apyanyathAbhAvo.avagata iti sandehAbhAvAtparIkShAnusaraNAnnivartate | nahi j~nAnasvarUpaM prAmANyaM cha viShayIkartuM svamahimnaiva shaknoti | tasya tu mAnasyA doShashaN^kayA prAmANyagrahaNashaktiH pratibaddhA | ato vyavasthaiva tatspR^ishati | na tvavadhAraNasyeShye | parIkShayA cha pratibandhe.apagate nijayaiva shaktyA prAmANyamavadhArayati | nachAsya vyutpAdanasyAprAmANye.api samatvAttasyApi svato grahaNamiti vAchyam.h | vaiShamyAt.h | prAmANyAvadhAraNe hi parIkShAyAH pratibandhakanivartakatvamAtraM shakyate.avadhArayitum.h | pratibandhakarahite sAkShiprAmANyagrahe tadanapekShaNAt.h | sahakAritve hi sarvatra tadapekShA syAt.h | tathA chAnavasthetyuktam.h | anyathA kAraNatvaM vyAhanyeta | na chAprAmANyaM kvApi parIkShA.anapekSheNa sAkShiNA nishchitacharam.h | yena pratibandhakanivartakatvaM tasyAH pratImaH | kintu sArvatrikatvAtkAraNatvameva | pratibandhakasya sArvatrikatvAdanyathAsiddhaM sArvatrikatvamiti chenna | pratibandhakanivR^ittAvaprAmANyaga(he)haNe cha parIkShAyAH kAraNatvopapatteH | evaM sati gauravamiti chenna | visheShAvadhAraNAyA ashakyatvasyaiva kalpakAbhAvAt.h | tathA.api parIkShAnvayavyatirekAnuvidhAyi(yaka)tvasyAnyathAsiddhiH shaN^kayata iti chet.h (na) | pratibandhakasya sArvatrikatAyAH kvApyadarshanenAnyathAsiddhishaN^kAnirAsAt.h | anyathA sarvatra sahakAriNAM tathAtvaM syAt.h | yadi j~nAnagrAhakAtiriktasya yathAkathamapi praveshAtprAmANyasya paratastvamiti matam.h, tadA sAkShiNa eva svataHprAmANyamanyasya parata ityaN^gIkAre.api na kashchidvirodha iti saN^kShepaH | vistarastu svayam.h(eva)AchAryeNa vakShyate |
atha matam.h | sAkShI pratyakShAdInAM prAmANyaM gR^ihNannapi katipayakAlakatipayapuruShasambandhibandhivaidhuryarUpameva | na punarasya kadAchitkutrApi kenApi svArthavyabhichAro na bhaviShyatItyevaMrUpam.h | tatkathaM tenAtyantikabAdhAbhAvalakShaNaM satyatvaM vishvasya 
siddhayedityata Aha- anyatheti ||
sAkShiNaH sarvathA bAdhavaidhurvalakShaNaprAmANyAgrAhakatve vishvasya pUrNasya brahmaNo.api prapaJNchavadvinivR^ittiH kiM kasmAnna shaN^kayate | nivartakAbhAvAdityata uktam.h- akasmAditi || nanu cha "satyaM j~nAnam.h' "tatsatyam.h' ityAdishrutyA, brahma na nivR^ittimat.h aj~nAnatatkAryAtiriktatvAt.h ityAdyanumAnena, niradhiShThAnakasyAsAkShikasya bhramasya, niravadhikasya bAdhasya chAdarshanAtprapaJNchAropAdyanyathA.anupapattyA, brahmaNassatyatA.avagamAttannetyata uktam.h- shrutIti || eteShAmapi pramANAnAM pratyakShAdInAmiva vinivR^ittiH shaN^kayatAmityarthaH | 
etaduktaM bhavati | "prapaJNchaviShayANAM pratyakShAdipramANAnAM nAtyantikaM prAmANyaM sAkShI gR^ihNAti | kintu tAtkAlikameva' iti vadanvaktavyaH | sAkShiNaH kimAtyantikaprAmANyagrahaNe shaktirastyuta nAsti | Adye kathaM prapaJNchaviShayANAM pratyakShAdInAM prAmANyamAtyantikaM na gR^ihNIyAt.h | dvitIye brahmaNaH satyatApratipAdakAnAM shrutyAdInAmapi nAtyantikaM prAmANyaM gR^ihNIyAt.h | tathAcha na brahmaNo.abAdhyatvamAtyantikaM siddhayet.h | tatashcha sAdhakabAdhakapramANAbhAvAttasyApi bAdhaH shaN^kayeta | evaMcha tajj~nAnamapi na tattvaj~nAnamiti na tadarthaH prayatnaH syAt.h | atha kvachichChaktiH kvachinneti brUyAttadA niyAmakaM vAchyamiti |
nanu yadi brahma bAdhArhaM syAttarhIyatA kAlena kuto na nivR^ittam.h | tasmAditaHpUrvaM bAdharahitatvAnnottaratrApi bAdhaH shaN^kayata iti chenna | uktottaratvAt.h | asyA apyupapatteH sAkShigrAhyapramANabhAvAyA AtyantikaprAmANyAsiddheH | anyathA prapaJNchagrAhiNAM pratyakShAdInAmapi tathAtvasyAnivAraNAt.h | vyavasthApakAbhAvAt.h | 
dUShaNAntaramAha- itaHpUrvamiti ||
tathAbhAvAt.h nivR^ittyabhAvAt.h | yadi brahmaNo nivR^ittinar shaN^kayata iti sambandhaH | tarhItyadhyAhAraH | gatirnivR^ittiH syAditi sheShaH | 
ayamAshayaH | itaHpUrvamanivR^ittatvAditi kiM brahmaNo nivR^ittyabhAve sambhAvanoktatAnumAnam.h | nAdyaH | sambhAvanAyA api saMshayarUpatvena shaN^kAnivAraNAsAmarthyAt.h | na dvitIyaH | tathA sati saMsR^iteravidyAyA nivR^ittyabhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | na hItaHprAN^.hmUlAvidyA nivR^ittA | anyathA tasyAmeva vyabhichArassyAditi |
kiJNcha shuktirajatAdikaM prAganivR^ittameva nivartate | nivR^ittasya nivR^ittyayogAt.h | ato viruddhatA cha | 
anyathetyAdyanyathA vyAkhyAyate | anyathA sAkShiNaH prapaJNchagrAhakapratyakShAdyAtyantikaprAmANyAgrAhakatve, vishvasya viyadAderuttarakShaNa eva nivR^ittirvinAshaH kiM na shaN^kayate | tathAcha sarvapravR^ittivilayaH syAt.h | parameshvarasaJNjihIrShAdyabhAvAdityata uktam.h- akasmAditi || (anu-1117 pR^iShThe draShyavyam.h |) nanvIshvarechChayaiva shrutismR^itItihAsapurANAni prapaJNchapralayaM pratipAdayanti, vishvavinAsho na nirhetuko vinAshatvAtpaTanAshavadityanumAnamapi | tatkathamevaM shaN^kayata ityata uktam.h- shrutIti || pramANAnAM nivR^ittirnAmAtyantikaprAmANyAbhAvaH | tAtparyaM pUvarvat.h | 
nanu prAgito na prapaJNcha(vi)layo.akasmAdabhUt.h | tatkathamuttaratrApi shaN^kayeta ityata (uktam.h) Aha- itaH pUrvamiti || kimatra yatpUrvaM nAbhUttaduttaratrApi na bhaviShyatIti vyAptiH, kiMvA yatpUrvaM na nirhetukaM vinaShyaM na taduttaratrApi tathA vinAshavaditi, yadvA yannirhetukaM na tadbhaviShyatIti vyAptiH, pUrvoktistu tadupapAdanAyeti | nAdyaH | saMsR^iteravidyAyA nivR^ittyabhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | na dvitIyaH | saMsAranivR^ittiprasaN^gAt.h | tathAhi | vidyA saMsAranivR^ittihetuH | sA.apyavidyAtmakatvAtsaMsR^itireva | nacha tasyA nivartakAntaramasti | tathAchAkasmAtkimapi na nivartata ityaN^gIkAre no saMsR^itergatiH | vidyA svayameva svanivR^ittiheturavidyAmAtravirodhitvAditi chenna | evaM tarhi prapaJNcho.apyuttarakShaNe (svayameva) nivartiShyata iti shaN^kA syAt.h | ata eva na tR^itIyo.apIti | 
uktamevArthaM vivR^iNoti- vAkyeti ||

iyamatra yojanA | "anAdimAyayA supto yadA jIvaH prabuddhayate | ajamanidramasvapnamadvaitaM buddhayate tadA' iti pUrvashloke.anAdimAyayA parameshvarapraj~nayA tadichChayA vA jIvajAtasya prakR^ityAdijaDAvR^itaj~nAnatvalakShaNaM suptatvaM tayaiva parameshvarAditattvaviShayaparokShaj~nAnalakShaNaM prabodhamabhidhAya aparokShaj~nAnamapyuktam.h | tena jIveshvarayorjaDeshvarayojarIvajaDayoshcha bhedAH pratipAditA | prabhorichChayA nigaDAdinA puruShe baddhe mukte vA bheda(traya)darshanAt.h |
