yadi cha jaDajIvabhedo nivarteta tadA jIvAnAM jaDatvApattyA mokShashAstravaiyarthyamityAdirUpeNa nivartetetyasyAniShyatvaM draShyavyam.h | na saMshaya itrata vyAptenirshchAyakamAha | evaM bhedapaJNchakasyAnAditAmupapAdya satyatAyAM pramANamAha- mAyAmAtramiti || yasmAdidaM prapaJNchashabdoktaM dvaitamuktarItyA mAyAmAtraM tasmAtsatyam.h | na hyavidyamAnamIshvarapraj~nAviShayo bhavati | bhrAntitvaprasaN^gAt.h | nApyavidyamAnaM kenApi rakShyate | atra dvayorbhAvo dvitA | tadIyo vargo dvaitam.h | sAmAnye napuMsakam.h | prapaJNchasambandhastu prakaraNAllabhyata iti j~nAtavyam.h | tarhyadvaitassarvabhAvAnAmityAdi kathamuktamityata Aha- advaitamiti || yadidaM parameshvarasyAdvaitatvaM(cha) visheShaNamuktaM na tat.h dvitIyavasturAhityAbhiprAyeNa | kintu paramArthataH | lyablopanimittA paJNchamI | uktamamarthamabhipretyeti | saptamyarthe vA tasiH | uttamArthaviShaya iti | bhedasatyatA.anaN^gIkAre bAdhakaM chAha- vikalpa iti || vikalpaH prakR^ito bhedo yadi kenachidaj~nAnAdinA kalpitaH syAttarhi chandrabhedavannivarteta | bAdhyeta | nacha bAdhyate | tasmAnna kalpitaH | kintu satya eveti | upasaMharati- upadeshAditi || tadevamupadeshAchChatyAdyanusAritvAt.h ayameva satAM vAdaH | yo bhedasatyatvAdiviShayaH | dvaitaM na vidyata iti tu tattve.aj~nAte sati bhavati | ato durvAda iti | 
adhunA pariNAmavAdinA vivartavAdinA cha pratij~nAdR^iShyA tAnuparodhAditi sUtrArthatayA gR^ihItAm.h "uta tamAdeshamaprAkSha' ityAdikAM shrutiM vyAkhyAti | 
tatra pariNAmavAdino vyAkhyAnam.h "uta tamAdeshamaprAkShaH, yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavatyamataM matamavij~nAtaM vij~nAtam.h' itrata jagato brahmapariNAmatayA tato.anantvAbhiprAyeNa tadvij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnaM pratij~nAtam.h | tatra sarvasya brahmopAdAnatAmajAnatA upAdAnopAdeyayorapi bhedaM manyamAnena shvetaketunA anyaj~nAne satyanyaj~nAnasya kvApyadarshanAt.h | "kathaM nu bhagavaH sa Adesho bhavati' iti chodite jagato brahmopAdAnatayA tadananyatvamupadekShyan.h laukikapratItisiddhaM kAraNAtkAryasyAnanyatvaM, tajj~nAnena tajj~nAnaM cha darshayati- "yathA somyaikena mR^itpiNDena sarvaM mR^iNmayaM vij~nAtaM syAt.h | vAchArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM mR^ittiketyeva satyam.h | yathA somyaikena lohamaNinA sarvaM lohamayaM vij~nAtaM syAt.h | vAchArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM lohamaNirityeva satyam.h yathA | somyaikena nakhanikR^intanena sarvaM kArShNAyasaM vij~nAtaM syAt.h | vAchA.a.arambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM kArShNAyasamityeva satyam.h' iti | yathaikamR^itpiNDAdipariNAmAnAM ghaTAdInAM tadananyayA tajj~nAnena j~nAtateti dR^iShyAntatrayArthaH | ananyatve kathaM kAryatvamityAshaN^kaya vyavahArArthamityAha- vAchA.a.arambhaNamiti | vAcheti ShaShThayarthe tR^itIyA | vAggrahaNaM samastendriyavyavahAropalakShaNam.h | vikAro.abhidheyo ghaTAdiH, nAmadheyaM tadabhidhAnamiti kumbhAdervAchyasya tadvAchakAnAM cha svarUpakAryavyapadeshAdibhedAtparasparaM bhedo vAstava ityuktam.h | etairhetubhiH parasparaM bhedashchetkAraNAdapi taireva bheda iti pUrvapakShaM niSheddhumAha- mR^ittiketyeva satyamiti || itishabdaH prakAravachanaH | yatprakAreNa yatsattayA mR^ittikA satI tatprakAreNaiva mR^iNmayaM satyam.h | nAshvamahiShAdivannairapekShyeNeti |
vivartavAdI tu vyAchaShye | ekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnaM pratij~nAya dR^iShyAntAkAN^kShAyAmuchyate- yathA somyeti || etaduktaM bhavati | ekena mR^itpiNDena paramArthato mR^idAtmanA vij~nAtena sarvaM mR^iNmayaM ghaTAdikaM mR^idAtmakatvAvisheShAdvij~nAtaM bhavet.h | yato vAchArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyam.h | vAchA kevalamastItyArabhyate | vikAro ghaTaH sharAva udaJNchanaM cheti | natu vastuvR^ittena vikAro nAma kashchidasti | nAmadheyamAtraM hyetadanR^itam.h | mR^ittiketyeva satyamityeSha brahmaNo dR^iShyAnta AmnAta iti | 
tatraikavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnapratij~nAnaM mR^itpiNDAdidR^iShyAntAshcha vikAravivartAbhiprAyA itye(vaM)tat.h na tAvadvAkyAtpratIyate | kintu vAchArambhaNamityupapAdakavAkyabalAditi vaktavyam.h | atastadeva prathamaM vyAkuvarnvAchArambhaNashabdArthamAha- vAchArabdhamiti ||
nanvArambhaNashabdo lyuDantaH | lyuT.h cha bhAve karaNAdhikaraNayoshcha vihito na karmaNi nacha "kR^ityalluTo bahulam.h' iti karmaNi lyuT.h | prabalaniyAmakamantareNa bahulagrahaNasya karmaNi vyAkhyAtumashakyatvAt.h | "na chArabhyasyArambhaNamiti yujyate shabdaH' iti svavachanavirodhAchcha | tatkathamArabdha iti vyAkhyAnamiti | maivam.h | bhAva evArambhaNashabdasyAN^gIkArAt.h | vAchA vAgindriyeNArambhaNamutpAdanaM yasyeti tR^itIyAyA aluk.h | "TApaM chApi halantAnAM yathA vAchA nishA dishA' iti vachanAt.h, vAchayA.a.arambhaNaM yasyeti vA bahuvrIhirayam.h | tasyArthakathanaM vAchAkhyamiti |
tushabdo.avadhAraNArtha uttaratra sambaddhayate |
vAchArambhaNashabdAdeva vikAratvalAbhAdvikAra iti punaruktaM syAdatastAtparyamAha- sAN^ketyeti || vAchArambhaNashabdena sAN^ketikaM nAmaiva vAchyaM syAt.h | avayavArthakathanaM tu vaishadyArthameva | yathA chaShye.aneneti chakShuriti nirvachanalabhyeti darshanakAraNatve chakShuShA pashyatIti noktArthatA | tasyAM dashAyAmavayavArthasyAvivakShitatvAt.h | tathAcha vAchArambhaNashabdo.api sAN^ketikaparyAya iti | 
vikArashabdArthamAha- vikR^itamiti ||
anena vikriyata iti vikAra iti karmaNi ghaJNityuktaM bhavati | vikR^itatvopapAdakamarthAntaraM chAha- vahniti || vividhaH mR^ittiketyeva satyamityasyArthamAha- tviti ||
satyashabdArtho nityamiti || tushabdo.avadhAraNe | Adishabdena lohamaNyAdergraDaNam.h | yanmR^ittiketyAdi saMskR^itaM nAmadheyam.h tadeva nityamiti sambandhaH | vaidikamiti tadupapAdanam.h | 
tatashchaivaM yojanA | vAchArambhaNaM sAN^ketikaM nAmadheyaM vikAra utpattimat.h | tata evAnityam.h | kutaH | bahuvidhatvAt.h | puruShechChAnusAreNAneka(vidha)prakAratvAt.h | mR^ittiketyAdinAmadheyaM vaidikatvAnnityamanAdi cheti | nacha vAchArambhaNaM vikAra iti liN^gavaiShamyadoShaH | nAmadheyavikArashabdayorniyataliN^gatvAt.h | vAchArambhaNashabdasya cha nAmadheyavisheShaNatvAt.h | visheShaNAnAM cha visheShyanighnatvAt.h | ata eva sAN^ketyamityeva vaktavye sAN^ketyanAmetyavochat.h | yadA tu vAchA yasyArambhaNaM tannAmadheyaM vikAro janimaditi, vAchA nAmnAmArambhaNaM vividhAkAraH, AkArAkAriNorabhedAt.h | vikAritvAdutpattivinAshavaditi yAvaditi vA granthAntaroktA yojanA, tadA(tu) liN^gavyatyAsashaN^kaiva nAstIti | 
nanu cha sAN^ketikAnAmanAmutpattivinAshavattvaM saMskR^itanAmnAmanAdinityatvaM kimarthamatrochyate | paramaprakR^ite brahmavij~nAnena 
sarvavij~nAne.avAntaraprakR^ite.asmAkamivadR^iShyAnte (vo)chopayogAbhAvAt.h | ato.asaN^gatatvAnnAyaM shrutyartha iti | maivam.h | yadyapi parasyeva nedaM dR^iShyAntopapAdakam.h | tathA.api brahmaj~nAnena sarvavij~nAne dR^iShyAntAntaratayopayokShyate | yathA tena tadvij~nAtaM syAditi, prakR^itAnuvR^itterityAshayavAnAha- prAdhAnyAditi ||
idamuktaM bhavati | kR^itakatvAdanityatvAchcha parApekShatvena sAN^ketikaM nAmApradhAnam.h | anAdinityatvAtparAnapekShatvena saMskR^itaM pradhAnam.h | tatra yathA prAdhAnyAtsaMskR^itaj~nAnamAtreNa sAN^ketikaM j~nAnaM bhavati | tajj~nAnena yatphalaM vidvadvayavahAragocharatvAdikaM tadbhavatIti yAvat.h | evamanityatvAdinA.apradhAnasya devatAkamarAdimishrasya sakalasyApi jagato j~nAnena yatphalaM tatsamastamapi nityatvAdinA pradhAnasya paramAtmano j~nAnAllabhyate | tatphale.antarbhavatIti | atra prAkR^itAj~no.apItyanena phalApekShayedamiti sUchitaM (bhavati) | evaM tarhyekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnamamukhyaM syAditi chet.h | satyam.h | nahi pareNApi tanmukhyaM vyAkhyAtuM shakyam.h | tathA sati dR^iShyamR^idaH puruShasya ghaTasharAvAdisaMsthAnavisheShAdijij~nAsA.abhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | pAmarA na hi vidvAniti vadanti, ataH sadbhirityuktam.h | evaM nityaparAtmaviditi vAkyasyoktAnusAreNa sheSho j~nAtavyaH | 
nanu satyashabdaH kathaM nityArthaH | rUDheryogasya chAbhAvAdityato yogaM tAvaddarshayati- sadAtanamiti ||
satyamitItyAvartanIyam.h | sadAtanaM satyamiti nirvachanena satyamiti padena nityamuchyata eva | na tUpacharyata iti | budhairvaiyAkaraNairiti nirvachanamUlaM sUchayati | sadAshabdAttatra bhava ityarthe "avyayAttyap.h' iti tyappratyaye kR^ite "sarvasya so.anyatarasyAM diH' ityatra yogavibhAgAtsadAshabdasya so.anyatarasyAM bhavati | sadAshabdAdbhavArthe taddhitA iti Dyapratyayo votpAdyaH | dakArasya cha takAraH | 
idAnIM rUDhimapi darshayati- prayogashcheti ||
uttaratrAShyame prapATha(ghaTTa)ke satyashabdasya nityatva eva prayogashchAstIti sambandhaH | tameva prayogaM darshayituM "yadainaM jarA.avApnoti pradhvaMsate vA kiM tato.a(syAti)vashiShyata iti sa brUyAnnAsya jarayaitajjIyarte na vadhenAsya hanyate etatsatyaM brahmapuram.h' iti vAkyamarthataH paThati- jareti ||
yadainaM dehaM jarA.avApnoti pradhvaMsate vA.ayaM dehaH, (tadA)tatastadasya dehasyAntargataH paramAtmA dahyamAnagehAntargatagaganavatkimatishiShyate kiMvA paTAdivannashyatIti pR^iShye, nAsya dehasya jarayA.ayaM paramAtmA jIryate, asya vadhena na hanyate, kintvetadbrahma pUrNatvAtpuraM satyaM nityamiti parihAro.abhidhIyate | itishabdasya pUrveNAnvayaH | atrApi satyashabdaH kuto nityArtha ityata Aha- nityatva eva hIti || 
atra satyashabdo nityArthashchetsaN^gachChate | vinAshasya prakR^itatvAt.h | tathyArthatAyAmasaN^gatiH | anR^itatAyA aprastutatvAditi hishabdArthaH | etadeva spaShyIkartumetatsatyaM brahmapuramityetAvati paThitavye pUrvavAkyamapi paThitam.h | pUrveNaiva sambandhaH | brahmaNo jarAvadhayorabhAve satyatvaM hetutvenochyata iti chet.h | na | tvayA brahmavyatirikta(sya)satyasyAnabhyupaga(me)tatvenAnvayAbhAvAt.h | jarAdyupetAnAM dehAnAmasatyatvAsyAsiddheH asatyAnAM cha shuktirajatAdInAM jarA.adyabhAvena vyatirekasyApyabhAvAt.h | nanu tathA.api vAchArambhaNavAkyaM trivAraM kasmAtpaThyate | shabdAntaraM dR^iShyAntIkartumiti brUmaH | tarhi ShaDete dR^iShyAntAH syuH | evamaivaitat.h | tathA sati saMskR^itashabdadR^iShyAntatrayamekatraiva vaktavyam.h | maivam.h | tattadabhidheyaprasaN^gAyattasya tadabhidhAnasya tadaiva vaktavyatvAt.h | tathA.api pratishabdaM dR^iShyAntIkaraNe.aparyavasAnaprasakterupalakShaNatve chaikenApi kR^itatvAchChabdatrayopAdAnamanupapannamiti chenna | mR^itpiNDAdidR^iShyAntatrayopAdAne.apyasya samAnatvAt.h | gahane prameye trayopAdAnaM na doShAya | kintu buddhivaishadyahetutayA guNayaiveti chet.h | samaM prakR^ite.apIti ||
evaM svamatena vAchArambhaNamityAdivAkyaM vyAkhyAya vivartavAda(di)vyAkhyAne doShamAha- vAchArambhaNamiti ||
uktam.h- uktiH shabda iti yAvat.h | vAchArambhaNamiti shabde mithyetivyAkhyAyamAne satIti sheShaH | tathAhi | kiM rUDhimAshritya vAchArambhaNamityasya mithyeti vyAkhyAnaM kriyate | kiMvA yogam.h | Adye rUDhij~nApakapramANAbhAvAdashrutakalpanam.h | athArabhyata ityArambhaNamiti dvitIyaH | tathA.api kR^idyoge ShaShThayAM prAptAyAM tR^itIyAN^gIkAre.ashrutakalpanam.h | lyuTaH karmaNi vidhAnAbhAvAchchAshrutakalpanameva | asminnapi pakShe mithyAtvasyAlAbhAdashrutakalpanam.h | vAchArabhyatvamAtreNa tathAtve brahmaNo.api tatprasaN^gAt.h | vAchA kevalamArabhyate vikAro na tu vastuvR^ittenAstIti vyAkhyAne mithyAtvaM labhyata iti chenna | yataH shrutyA vAchArambhaNamityevokte kevalashabdaprakShepeNa mithyeti vyAkhyAne.ashrutakalpanameveti |
dUShaNAntaramAha- punaruktiriti || 
itishabdo.atrAdhyahAryaH | AgAmino vA kAkAkShinyAyenobhayatra sambandhaH | nAmadheyamityetannAmadheyamAtraM hyetadanR^itamiti pareNa vyAkhyAtam.h | tasya vAchArambhaNamityanenaiva gatArthatvAnnAmadheyamiti punaruktiH syAt.h | atha vikAro nAmadheyaM cha dvayamapi vAchArambhaNamiti vyAkhyAnaM, tathA.api vikArashabdenaivAbhidheyAbhidhAnayorgrahaNasambhavAnnAmadhayemiti punaruktireveti | tannAmarUpAbhyAM vyAkriyata ityAdishruteH | 
doShAntaramAha- itItyasyeti ||
mR^ittikAyAH satyatvaM hi parasya vivakShitam.h | tatra mR^ittikaiva satyeti vakta(vyam.h)vye itishabdastu nirarthaka eva | sa hi kvachitpadArthaviparyAsakR^it.h, kvachiddhetau, kvApyevamityarthe, kutrachidAdishabdArthe, kvachitprakArArthe, kvachitparisamAptau | na chAtrai(te)vamAdiShvanyatamenArthenArthavAn.h | asmAkaM tu "shabdAdathare sampratyayaH' iti mR^ittikArthe prApte tatparihAreNa shabdasvarUpagrahaNArthaM tadupapattiH | pariNAmavAdino.api kR^idyoge tR^itIyAyA aN^gIkR^itatvAt.h lyuTaH karmaNi vyAkhyAtatvAdvAchArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyamityeteShAM padAnAmanvayAbhAvena padAntarAdhyAhArasyeShyatvAdashrutakalpanam.h, nAmadheyasyApi vikAragrahaNena grahaNasambhavAtpunaruktiH, itishabdasya nirarthakatA cheti sphuTatvAnnoktam.h | nanu tenetishabdaH prakAravachana ityuktam.h | tatkathaM nirarthakatA | uchyate | kAryakAraNayorbhedashaN^kAnirAsArthaM hIdamuchyate | tatra yatsattayA mR^ittikA satI tayaiva mR^iNmayaM satyamiti vyAchakShANena vaktavyam.h, keyaM sattA vivakShiteti | svarUpasattA chetsAdhyAvishiShyatA | yo hi kAryakAraNayorbhedaM manyate, sa kathaM kAraNasvarUpeNaiva kAryaM svarUpavadityaN^gIkuryAt.h | atha sAmAnyasattA | sA.anaikAntikI | nahi mahiShasattayA sannashvo mahiShAnna bhidyate | atha mR^ittikAsattAdhInasattAkaM mR^iNmayamiti vivakShitamiti, tathA.api kulAlAdisattAdhInasattAkamapi bhavatItyanaikAntyameva | viruddhaM cha(chai)tat.h | yadyadadhInaM tadeva taditi | ato vivakShitasAdhanAnupayogitvAditishabdasya tanmate.api nirarthakataiveti | 
idAnIM yathA somyetyAdIni dR^iShyAntavAkyAni svamatena vyAkariShyanparakIyavyAkhyAyAM tAvaddoShamAha- eka iti ||
padasamuchchaye prathamashchashabdaH | itishabdasya pratyekaM sambandhaH | vaiyarthyaM vigatArthatvaM viruddhArthatvaM cha | evashabdena vaiyarthyasyAparihAryatAmAha | chashabdasya vivartavivakShAyAM chetyarthaH | jagato brahmavikAratvena tadAropitatvena chaikavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAne vivakShite mR^idA vij~nAtayA mR^iNmayaM vij~nAtaM syAt.h | lohena vij~nAtena lohamayaM vij~nAtaM syAt.h | kR^iShNAyasA vij~nAtena kAShNarAyasaM vij~nAtaM syAdityetAvatA pUrNatvAttrayANAmekashabdAnAM piNDamaNinakhanikR^intanashabdAnAM sarvashabdAnAM cha vigatAthartvaM syAt.h | sarvamR^iNmayAdInAmekamR^itpiNDAdivikAratvAbhAvAdviruddhArthatA cha syAt.h | AropitatvaM tvekasyApi mR^iNmayasyaikasminmR^itpiNDe nAsti | kutaH sarvasya | yuktyA samathyarta iti chet.h | tarhi vivAdapadatvena dR^iShyAntatA.anupapattiH | "laukikaparIkShakANAM yasminnarthe buddhisAmyaM sa dR^iShyAntaH' iti hi nyAyavidaH | kintu ghaTAdInAmabAdhitapratyakShAdisiddhatvena yuktirevAbhAsabhUteti paramANupuJNjavAdanirAse vakShyate | Aropitatve.api naikasminsarvamityekAdipadAnAM vaiyarthyameva | 
nanvakeneti paramAkAraNasyaikatvaM piNDeneti kAryAbhimukhyaM sarvamiti kAryanAnAtvaM vivakShitam.h | ataH kathaM vaiyarthyamiti | maivam.h | dArShyAntikavAkye tadvivakShAyAmatra vaiyarthyAparihArAt.h | 
api chAdyayordR^iShyAntayoH kAryakAraNabhAvamAtramasti | kintvekAdipadavaiyarthyameva | idantu sarvathA nopapadyate, yathA somyaikena nakhanikR^intaneneti | nakhanikR^intanasyAntyAvayavitvena kArShNAyasAntaraM prati kAraNatvasyaivAsambhavAt.h | kimvekasya sarvaM pratItyAha- nacheti || 
sarvaM cheti dvitIyachashabdasambandhaH | 
yadyatra dR^iShyAntatraye na vikAravivartavivakShA kiM tarhi vivakShitamityata Aha- ata iti ||
arthAntarasya dUShitatvAdityarthaH | chashabdAvitarotarasamuchchaye | tushabdena nityatvaM vishinaShyi | nityatvaM prAdhAnyopapAdakameva na tu svatantramekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnasyeti | mR^itpiNDAdidR^iShyAntatrayaM sAdR^ishyaviShayam.h | vAchArambhaNamityAdi tu prAdhAnyaviShayamiti vivektavyam.h | vAchArambhaNadR^iShyAntasya pUrvameva vyAkhyAtatvAtkiM punarvachaneneti chenna | buddhayArohArthamuktasyApyanuktena sahaikena vAkyenoktisambhavAdityAshayenoktam.h- ukteti || sAdR^ishyAdekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnamAchAryeNAnyatra vyutpAditamatrAnusandheyam.h | tathA mR^itpiNDAdidR^iShyAntAnAmavAntarabhedo.apIti | 
nanvasminnapi pakShe "sadeva somyedamagra AsIt.h' ityAderuttaragranthasya saN^gatyabhAvo doShaH | asmAkaM tu kAryakAraNabhAvAdiprapaJNchArthatvena astyupayoga ityata Aha- prAdhAnyeti || 
Adipadena pralaye.avasthAnaM trivR^itkaraNaM jIvarUpeNa praveshanamityAdikaM gR^ihyate | prAdhAnyAdbrahmaj~nAnena sarvaj~nAnasya phalaM bhavatItyukte, kutastasya prAdhAnyamityAshaN^kAyAM, tatpratipattyarthaM sR^iShyayAdeH pratipAdaka eva granthavistaraH pravR^itto.ataH kathamasaN^gatiriti | chashabdo.avadhAraNe | na tUpAdAnatvAdipratipattyarthamiti | na hyupAdanAM prekShApUrvaM kAryaM karoti | nApyadhiShThAnamadhyastam.h | eSha cheti vA sambandhaH | tena "apAgAdagneragnitvam.h' ityAdyapi parasya brahmaNaH prAdhAnyapratipattyarthamevetyuktaM bhavati | tathAchoktaM bhAShye | 
vivartamatanirAkaraNamupasaMharati- tasmAditi ||
kenApi mArgeNeti || brahmAvidyApekShayA vA, jIvAvidyApakSheNa vA, ekajIvamatena vA, anekajIvamatena vA, svapakShasAdhanena vA, parapakShanirAsena vA, yuktiparyAlochanayA vA, shrutipayarAlochanayA vA, vichAritamiti sheShaH | na bhavet.h upapannamityadhyAhAraH | tataH kimityata Aha- taditi || 
tat.h vivartamatam.h | tasmAdita vA | tasyaiva vivaraNaM asaN^khayAtadoShetaM yasmAditi | heyameva tat.h | natu taduktarItyA sUtrArtho grAhyaH | etena paramatanirAkaraNasyAsaN^gatirapi nirastA veditavyA | 
yadyuktAtiriktadoShAH santi | tarhi dUShaNAbhidhAnAya pravR^ittairvaktavyAH | kimuparameNetyata Aha- asaN^khayatveneti ||
doShANAmatibahutvena kAMshchiduktvA keShAJNchidupalakShaNe(Natve)naivoparantavyam.h | upalakShaNaM chaitAvatA.api bhavatItyuparamyata iti | sarve.api vaktavyAH, kimupalakShaNatvenetyata uktam.h- grantheti || granthAdhikye hi shrotR^INAM pravR^ittirna syAt.h | tathAcha kR^itamapyakR^itaM syAditi bhayAdapItyarthaH |

ekavAkyatA(di)siddhaye prathamAdhyAyArthasaN^gatatvena dvitIyAdhyAyArthaM vivakShurabuddhisthena saN^gaterdarshayitumashakyatvAt.h prathamAdhyAyArthaM tAvadanuvadati- ukta iti ||
(sakala)jagajjanmAdinimittakAraNe sArvajj~nasarvaishvaryAdyanantaguNaparipUrNe.avidyAdyavadyagandhavidhure pare brahmaNi nArAyaNe svaravarNapadavAkyamahAvAkyarUpasya samastasya shAstrasya, sAkShAtparamamukhyayA vR^ittyA natu lakShaNayA, tathA mahAtAtparyeNa natu pArArthyena samanvayaH prathame.adhyAye samarthita ityarthaH | 
yadyapi samanvayashabdenaiva sAkShAdityartho labhyate | tathA.api parakIyasaMshabdavyAkhyAnanirasane.avahitairbhavitavyamiti sUchanAya tadvayAkhyAnamidaM kR^itamityadoShaH | athavA samanvayashabdena mukhyayA vR^ittyA.anvayaH pratIyate | paramamukhyayA tu vR^ittyA anvayaM darshayituM sAkShAdityuktam.h | yadvA na pradhAnaparamANvAdinirAsanena upAdAnatvAdipratipAdanena cha paramparayA kintu sAkShAdevetyanenAchaShye | 
evaM prathamAdhyAyArthamabhidhAya tatsaN^gatatvena dvitIyAdhyAyArthamAha- avirodha iti ||

nirAshrayatvAt.h | virodhasphUrtAveva tadabhAvasAdhanasyAvasaro netarathA | aprAptapratiShedhAyogAt.h | ato.atItAdhyAyArthasya kAraNatvametadadhyAyArthasya kAryatvaM nishchIyate | athavA shrutisamanvayenopapAdito.apyartho na tAvachChrotR^INAM dR^iDhanirUDho bhavati, yAvadatra pratIte virodhAbhAvo na sAdhyate | virodhena shrutInAmevAprAmANyashaN^kanAt.h | tathA chAnupapAditakalpa evApadyate | virodhAbhAvasAdhane tu bhavatyeva dR^iDhanirUDhaH | yathoktam.h | "vimR^ishya pakShapratipakShAbhyAmarthAvadhAraNaM nirNayaH' iti | ato viparItakAryakAraNabhAvalakShaNA anayossaN^gatiH |

tasyAvirodhasya | nirdhAraNe ShaShThI | Adau prathamapAde | avirodhaH sAdhyata ityanuvartate | chaturvidhasya tasyetyanuvAdAtsa chaturvidha iti labhyate |

prathamAdhikaraNe visheShamAha- tatrApIti ||
apipadamAdAvityasyAnukaSharNArtham.h | tatra yuktivirodhAbhAvapratipAdake.api pAda ityanauchityashaN^kAsUchanArthaM vA | chashabdenAvirodhaH sAdhyata ityetadanukR^iShyate | smR^iteH pAshupatAdikAyAH | yadyapi smR^iterityasya na naJNarthena sambandho ghaTate virodhashcha samAse guNabhUtaH | tathA.api buddhayA viviktena tena sambandhaH sambhavati |

ayamihAbhisandhiH pUrvapakShiNaH | shrutivirodhena smR^itInAmaprAmANyamabhilaShatA prabaladurbalatve sarvathA samarthanIye | anyathA.atiprasaN^gAt.h | na tAvatprAmANyakAraNabhAvAbhAvAbhyAM prAbalyadaurbalye | prAmANyasya svatastvenAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | vaiparItyAchcha | vAkyaprAmANye hi kAraNaM vakturAptatvam.h | vaktArashcha smR^itInAmAptAH | na shruteH | apauruSheyatvenAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | ata eva samUlatvanirmUlatvAbhyAm.h | smR^itInAmAptimUlatvAt.h | shrutestadabhAvAt.h | nApi kR^ittimatvAkR^itrimatvAbhyAm.h | svarUpato.aprayojakatvAt.h | uktarItyA vaiparItyAchcha | tadidamuktamAptai rudrakapilakamalAsanAdibhiH uktamarthaM shivAdInAM jagatkAraNatvAdikaM, pipIlikAlipinibhA buddhipUrvapraNayahInA, shrutiH, kathaM vArayet.h na kathamapIti | 
nanvaudumbarIM spR^iShTvodgAyedityAdishrutiviruddhAnAmaudumbarI sarvA veShyayitavyetyAdismR^itInAmaprAmANyamupalabdhaM tathA.atra syAt.h | na syAt.h | vaiShamyAt.h | shrutimUlatayA.abhimatA hi tAH smR^itayo.atastAsAM mUlashrutyanumApakatvena prAmANyamiShyam.h | nacha shrutiviruddhAyAH smR^itermUlashrutyanumApakatvaM sambhavatItyaprAmANyameva yuktam.h | yathA.a.aha jaiminiH "virodhe tvanapekShaM syAdasati hyanumAnam.h' iti | nachaivaM prakR^ite | pAshupatAdismR^itInAM shivAdipratyakShamUlatvena shrutimUlatvAbhAvAt.h | tadidamAha- pratyakShato dR^iShTveti || nanu tarhi smR^itInAmuktarItyA sAvakAshatvAnniravakAshashrutivirodhenAprAmANyamastu | maivam.h | vaiparItyAt.h | smR^itayo hi vispaShyavAdinyo na vivakShitArthAtprachyAvanamarhanti | shrutayastvasphuTa(spaShya)vikShiptavAdinyo.avyavasthitAlaukikashAbdalakShaNaviShayA ashakyAdhyayanAnantAparipUrNavAkyarUpA nArthavisheShaniShThA lakShyante | ata eva bhavatAM mImAMsAyAsaH | etadapyuktaM prakarSheNoktamiti | vispaShyamuktamityarthaH | 
pipIlikAlipinibheti cha | asphuTe(spaShye)tyarthaH |

nanu ye viruddhe pramANe na tayoH sAmyam.h | shuktirajataj~nAnayostadabhAvadarshanAt.h | ye cha same na tayorvirodhaH | paTashuklo dIrghashchetyatra tadabhAvAt.h | tatkathaM pAshupatAdismR^iteH satpratipakShatvasambhavaH | sambhave.api jitaM pareNa | siddhAntanirNayasyAyogAdityata Aha- mAnamiti || ubhayatra dvayossmaraNayormadhye yatsamaM saha mayA mUlapramANena vartate, tadeva mAnamanyadapramANam.h | etaduktaM bhavati | visheShAnirdhAraNAyAmeva satpratipakShatvam.h | vastutastu samUlaM mAnamanyadamAnamiti | nanu samUlatvena prAmANyAvadhAraNe prAmANyasya paratastvApattiH | maivam.h | parasparavirodhenAprAmANyashaN^kAprAptau samUlatvena tadapanayanAt.h | tathobhayatra smaraNe yatpaJNcharAtrAdismaraNaM samaM samUlapramANaM saMvAdipamANAntaropetaM cha, tadeva mAnaM bhavenna tu pAshupatAdikam.h, mUlAdyabhAvAt.h | ato noktadoSha iti yojyam.h | vakShyete hi shrutimUlatvatatsaMvAditve cha paJNcharAtrAdInAm.h | nanu kathaM pAshupatAdismR^itInAM nirmUlatvAt.h | yAvatA pashupatiprabhR^itInAmAptistatra mUlamuditetyata Aha- na cheti ||

atha te na tathA, kintvayogyajanavyAmohanArthamiti chet.h | prakR^ito.api na tatheti kuto nishchitam.h | nishchayopAyasyetaratrApi tulyatvAt.h |

evaM nyAyasAmyAbhAvena pratibandI mochitA | yadapi pratibandImAdadAnasya vivakShitam.h | yathA cha paJNcharAtrAdiprAmANyamabhilaShatA phalavyabhichArasyAdhikArAdivaikalyanibandhanatA kalpyA tathA.ahamapi pAshupatAdismR^itiShu kalpayiShyAmIti, tadayuktaM vaiShamyAdityAha- adhikAro hIti ||

vedavAkyamiti sheShaH | ayamarthaH | bodhakatvena khalu karaNAnAM prAmANyaM doShAttu, kadAchidapanIyate | vedavAkyaM cha bodhakatvena vAdiprativAdisammatam.h | anyathA phalavyabhichAro.api tatra(sya) na syAt.h | vAkye cha prAmANyasyApavAdakA doShA abodhakatvaviparItabodhakatvAdayaHsarve.api vaktR^idoShanibandhanA eva | anvayavyatirekAbhyAM tadavagamAt.h | vedavAkyaM cha nityatvAdapauruSheyatvAtpuruShadoShanibandhanaiH sarvadoShairvarjitaM svata eva prAmANyamApnoti | prAmANye cha nishchite sati phalavyabhichArasya sAmagrIvaikalyaM vA pratibandhakasadbhAvo vA kAraNaM kalpayiShyate | anyathA siddhAnanyathAsiddhayorananyathAsiddhasya balavattvAditi |
atraite prayogA bhavanti | vedaH pramANaM bodhakatve sati viparItabodhakatvAtsampratipannavat.h | vimato viparItabodhako na bhavati anAptApraNItavAkyatvAtsampratipannavAkyavat.h | vimato anAptapraNIto na bhavati apauruSheyatvAdvayomavat.h | vimataH phalavyabhichAro vaikalyAdinibandhano bhava(vitumarha)ti pramANasiddhaphalavyabhichAratvAt.h charakAdyuktaphalavyabhichAravaditi |

ye tu svayUthyA vedaprAmANyamaN^gIkR^ityApi tannityatAM nAnumanyante tAnprati sUtrasUchitAbhiH shrutibhistAmupapAdayati- virUpeti ||
anena "tasmai nUnamabhidyave vAchA virUpa nityayA | vR^iShNe chodasva suShyutim.h' iti shrutimupAdatte | 
atra vAcho nityatvamuchyate | na vedasya | tadapi bahukAlInatvaM bhaviShyatItyato "nityayA.anityayA staumi brahma tatparamaM padam.h' iti "shrutirvAva nityA.anityA vAva smR^itayo yAshchanyA vAchaH' iti shrutimupAdatte- nityayeti ||   Vyasa-(9) 
vyAkhyAnAntaranirAsAya nityayetyetatsadA vidyamAnayeti vyAkhyAtam.h | vAkyasheShe hi bahukAlInA api smR^itIranityapakShe nikShipya shrutimeva nityAmAha | pauruSheyatAmapi shrutayo.abhidadhatIti chenna | Aptoktatvasya duravadhAraNatAyAH prAguktatvena pauruSheyatve prAmANyAvadhAraNAnupapattiprasaN^gena durbalatvAt.h | prAmANyasya svatastvenApauruSheyatve.api kAraNAbhAvAtprAmANyaM na syAditi prasaN^gasyAbhAsatvAt.h | prabalashrutyanusAreNa tattatpuruShapravartitatvameva tAsAmartho.avagantavyaH | tathAcha "R^ichaH sAmAni jaj~nire' "R^igveda evAgnerajayata' ityAdyupapannaM bhavati | na hyekaM vAkyamanekakartR^ikamapi sambhavati | sambhavati tvanekapravartitamiti | 
yadapi pipIlikAlipivadabuddhipUrvakatvAdaprAmANyaM shruteriti, tannirAkaroti- pipIliketi ||
cho yasmAdityarthe | bodhakatvasamuchchaye vA | tasmAt.h dR^iShyAntasya sAdhyavikalatvAdasadanumAnamiti sheShaH | na kevalaM shrutiH kintu pipIlikAlipirapItyaperarthaH | 
aprAmANyaM khalu pipIlikAliperabodhakatvena vA syAdviparItabodhakatvena vA | nAdyaH | anubhavaviruddhatvAt.h | anyathA puruShaliperapyabodhakatvaM syAt.h | tathAcha tadvaiyarthyamApadyeta | api chaivaM satyAkAshAdikamevodAhriyeta tatkiM pipIlikAlipigaveShaNayA | na dvitIyaH | taddhi balavatpramANavirodhataH kalpanIyamanyathA.atiprasaN^gAt.h | nacha pipIlikAlipibodhite.arthe pramANavirodho.asti | ataH kathamasAvapramANaM syAt.h H 
syAdetat.h | lipistAvanna pramANaM pR^ithak.h | anupramANatritvAbhyupagamAt.h | nacha pratyakShAgamayorantarbhavati | atallakShaNatvAt.h | 
ato.anumAnameveti vAchyam.h | tachcha lekhakabuddhisthashabdaviShayaM vA tadavabuddhArthaviShayaM vA syAt.h | na chaitatpipIlikAlipau sambhavati | pramANabAdhitatvAttatkathamasau pramANamiti | maivam.h | tathA satyeDamUkaliperapyaprAmANyaprasaN^gAt.h | bhavatu sA.apramANamitarA tvanumAnamiti chenna | eDamUkaliperapi sAMvyAvahArikatvadarshanAt.h | kiJNchetaratrApyanumAne kimeDamUkavyAvR^ittyarthaM kimapi visheShaNamupAdeyamuta neti vAchyam.h | nAdyaH | sandigdhAsiddhiprasaN^gAt.h | nirNItalekhakaiva lipiranumAnamiti chenna | anirNItalekhakAyA api sAMvyAvahArikatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | eDamUkalipAvanaikAntyAt.h | atha mUlalekhakabuddhisthashabdArthAnumAne na ko.api doSha iti matam.h | tadapi na | pipIlikAlipAvanaikAntyAt.h | tadvayAvartane cha sandigdhAsiddheH | nahi pipIlikAlipeH puruShaliperasti kashchidvisheSho yena neyaM pipIlikAlipiriti nishchinuyAt.h | tasmAtpuruShalipirapi padamiva padArthasya varNAnAM smaraNahetureShyavyA | tatsamaM pipIlikAlipAvapi | smR^iteshcha pramitatvaM vakShyAmaH | 
nanu pramAtve.api smR^iterna taddhetumAtrasya prAmANyam.h | pramAtrAdInAmapi tatprasaN^gAt.h | kintu sAdhakatamasyaiva | tachcha mana eveti siddhAntaH | lipidarshanAdikaM tu saMskAro dvedhAbhidhasahakArisampAdanenaiva charitArthamiti kathaM tasya prAmANyam.h | maivam.h | arthasannikarShalakShaNAvAntaravyApArasahitaM hIndriyaM pratyakShaM nendriyamAtram.h | manasashcha smaraNodaye saMskArodbodha evArthasannikarShaH | tathAcha chakShuSha ivArthopasarpaNatatsaMyogasahitasya prAmANyamevaM lipidarshanatadudbuddhasaMskArasahitasyaiva manasa iti kathaM na lipeH prAmANyam.h | kevalAyAstu nAstIti chet.h | shruterapi tannAN^gIkriyata eveti |
nanvatra pramANashabdo bhAvasAdhano vA syAtkAraNasAdhano vA | Adye pipIlikAlipiH pramANamiti sAmAnAdhikaraNyaM na syAt.h | dvitIye tu pramANIti bhavitavyam.h | kathaM vedAH pramANaM smR^itiH pramANamiti | pramANamiti sAmAnyenoddishya vedAditvavidhAnAt.h | anyathA tatrApi daurghaTyameveti | maivam.h | bhAvasAdhanatvAbhyupagamAt.h | sAmAnAdhikaraNyaM tu bhAktamiti | 
nanu cha shruteH samyaganubhavasAdhanatvena prAmANyamiShyaM natu smArakatvena | tathAcha na shrutiH samyaganubhavasAdhanabuddhipUrvakatvAtpipIlikAlipivadityanumAsyata ityata Aha- yatheti ||
yathA.abuddhipUrvakamapyekenolUkena kR^itamanekakAkanAshanamashvatthAmno.ahameka evAnekAnvadhiShyAmItyasyArthasya bodhakaM samyaganubhavaM prati sAdhanaM jAtam.h | tathA shrutirabuddhipUrvA.api samyaganubhavasAdhanam.h | etaduktaM bhavati | abuddhipUrvakatvaM kimanAditvaM vivakShitam.h, sAditve.api buddhijanyatvAbhAvo vA pratipAdyAtharbuddhipUrvakatvAbhAvo vA.anenaitadevaM pratipAdayiShyAmItyabhisandhipUrvakatAvaidhuryaM vA | nAdyaH | pipIlikAlipAvabhAvAt.h | gaganameva dR^iShyAnto bhaviShyatIti chet.h | tathA.api shruteranAditvasya pareNAnaN^gIkR^itatvenAsiddheH | na dvitIyaH | utpadyamAnaM buddhijanyameveti mayA.aN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | na tR^itIyachatutharau | ulUkakR^itavyApAre vyabhichArAditi | yadyapi pratyakShe vyabhichAro.atra vaktuM shakyate | tathA.api j~nAtakAraNasajatIyatvena shakyaparihAro.asAviti noditaH | anumAnamAtre suvacho.api chetanavyApAraviShayasya tathAbhUta eva shAkune pradarshayitumuchita iti na pradarshitaH | nanu shAkunamarthavisaMvAdyapi dR^ishyate | satyam.h | yattu pramANAviruddhaM tadvayabhichArasthalaM bhaviShyatIti bhAvenoktam.h- aviruddhamiti || shAkunamAtre vyabhichArasya darshayituM shakyatve.apyAgamikatvena visaMvAdAnarhatayedamudAhR^itam.h | 
nanvAseti katham.h | asterbhUrityasya nityatvAt.h | vibhaktipratirUpakaM chAvyayaM bhavatIti vachanAdavyayametaditi na doShaH | vibhaktipratirUpakamityuchyate | nachaivaM vibhaktirasti | na nAsti | AmantAnuprayogasya vidyamAnatvAt.h | 
nanvevaM tarhi prayujyate | shrutirna samyaganubhavasAdhanaM shabdatve satyabuddhipUrvakatvAditi | yadvA shrutirnAgamo.abuddhipUrvakatvAditi | abuddhipUrvakatvaM cha vivakShitArthatattvaj~nAnapUrvakatvAbhAvaH | Adya(syApi)sya pipIlikAlipAvapraveshe.apyunmattavAkyaM dR^iShyAnto bhaviShyati | na chonmattavAkyamapi pramANaM pramANaviruddhatvAdityata Aha- viruddhaM tviti ||
pramANaviruddhaM yadunmattavAkyaM tat.h pramANavirodhAdeva bAdhitamayathArthamiti yAvat.h | na tUktahetubhyAmiti | sopAdhikatAmanenAchaShye | ata evAptApraNItavAkyatvaheturapyapAstaH | ayamabhisandhiH | na tAvatsamyaganubhavasAdhanatvAbhAvo j~nAnasAdhanatvAbhAvena | j~nAnasAdhanatvasyobhayasiddhatvAt.h | nApi smR^itisAdhanatvena | ananubhUtaviShayatvasammateH | tato viparItabodhakatvenaiveti vAchyam.h | evaM dvitIyaprayoge.api na tAvadanAgamatvamashabdatvena | shabdatvasyobhayasammatatvAt.h | tasmAdayathAthartveneti vaktavyam.h | evaM tR^itIyaprayoge.api sAdhyaniShkaSharH kartavyaH | tathAcha tatra pramANabAdhitatvamupAdhiH | yadvA.anubhavasAdhanatvAvachChinne prathamasAdhye, vAkyatvAvachChinne dvitIyasAdhye bodhakatvAvachChinne tR^itIye chAyamupAdhiriti |
nanvasyopAdheryadayathArthaM tatpramANaviruddhamiti sAdhyavyApakatve.api sAdhanAvyApakatvaM kathamityata Aha- virodheti ||
pakShIkR^itAyAM shrutAvuktasAdhanasadbhAve.api pramANavirodhasyAdasharnAt.h | sAdhanAvyApakatvamiti sheShaH | atra virodhAbhAvAditi vaktavye.adarshanAdityuktaM virodhAbhAvasAdhanArthamiti draShyavyam.h | 
kimato yadyevaM pramANaviruddhatvamupAdhiriti chet.h | upAdheH pratipakShonnAyakatvasya vakShyamANatvenAnumAnAnAM satpratipakShatvamityAshayenAha- tasmAditi ||
yasmAtpramANaviruddhatvamayathArthatvasya vyApakaM vyAvR^itaM cha pakShIkR^itAdvedAt.h | vyApakanivR^ittau vyApyanivR^ittiravashyambhAvinI | tasmAdvedaprAmANyameShyavyam.h | ayamatra prayogaH | vedo nAyathArthaH pramANAviruddhatvAtpratyakShavat.h | yadvA vedo yathArtho bodhakatve sati pramANAviruddhatvAtpratyakShavat.h | evaM vedaH samyaganubhavasAdhanamanubhavasAdhanatve sati pramANaviruddhatvAtpratyakShavat.h | veda Agamo vAkyatve sati pramANAviruddhatvAtsampratipannavaditi | evaM vAkyatvAvachChinne sAdhye.anAptapraNItatvamupAdhistadviparyayeNa cha pratipakSho.abhidheya iti | 
astvevaM vedaprAmANyam.h | paJNcharAtrAdismR^itInAM tu katham.h | nahi tA apyapauruSheyAH | yena prAmANyamavadhArya phalavyabhichAramanyathA neShyAma ityata Aha- tanmUlatvAditi || 
prAmANyamiShyata iti sambandhaH | yadyapi bhagavadrachitAnAM vedA(da)rthamupalabhya rachitatvaM vedamUlatvaM nAsti | tasya svataH sarvaj~natvam.h | tathA.api tamanusR^itya rachitatvaM tanmUlatvamiha vivakShitamiti noktadoShaH | ayamatra prayogaH | paJNcharAtrAdismR^itiH pramANaM pramANamUlatvAtpramANasaMvAditvAtsampratipannavaditi | yadvA vimataM pramANaM vedasaMvAditvAtparAbhyupagatArhiMsAdivAkyavat.h | AptavAkyatvamupAdhiriti chet.h (na) | pratyakShAdau sAdhyAvyApanAt.h | vAkyatvAvachChinnasAdhyavyApakatvAdadoSha iti chenna | tathA.api vedetaravAkyatvAvachChinnasAdhanenopAdheH pakShe sAdhanasaulabhyAt.h | sati chaivaM smR^itInAM prAmANye tadbalena phalavyabhichAro.apyanyathayitavya iti |
nanu choktArthaviruddhavAdInyapi smR^itItihAsapurANAnyupalabhyante | teShAM prAmANyasAdhane cha bahuviplavaH syAdityata Aha- virodha iti ||
pUrveNaivAnvayaH | yAsAM smR^itInAM sarvathA pramANavirodho nAsti tAsAmeva pakShIkaraNAnna kashchiddoSha ityAshayaH | nanvevaM sati vedamUlatvopanyAso vyarthaH | j~nAnajanakAnAmavashyAN^gIkaraNIyena virodhAbhAvenaiva prAmANyasiddheriti chenna | phalavyabhichAralakShaNavirodhadarshanenAsiddhiprasaN^gAt.h | prAmANyena tadapanayane chetaretarAshrayatvApAtAt.h | vedamUlatvena tu prAmANye siddhe na ko.api doSha iti |
aprAmANyaprayojakasya pramANavirodhasyAbhAvAnna shrutismR^ityoraprAmANyamityuktam.h | tadayuktam.h | shrutyAdyukta(sya) IshvarasArvaj~nAderIshvaro na sarvaj~naH puruShatvAt.h | yaj~nadattavat.h | ityAdyanumAnaviruddhatvAdityata Aha- virodho.apIti || 
prakR^itasambandhArtho.apishabdaH | yachChabdo.adhyAhAryaH | virodhAdeva bAdhitamityaprAmANyaprayojakatayokto virodho.api sa eva yaH pratyakSheNAgamena vA syAt.h | na punaranumAnena | ayamabhisandhiH | aprAmANyaprayojakatayA yadasmAbhirabhihitaM tatpakShe.apyupapAdayituM khalu parasyAyaM prayatnaH | asmAbhishcha pratyakShAgamavirodha eva tathA.abhipreto nAnumAnavirodhaH | tathAcha pakShe tad.hvyutpAdanaM prakR^itAsaN^gatameva | svatantrAnumAnavirodhaM tUttaratra nirAkariShyati sUtrakR^iditi |
nanu pramANavirodha evAprAmANye prayojako.astu kiM pratyakSheNAgamena veti visheShaNena | tathA choktanumAnavirIdhAdvedAderaprAmANyamiti | maivam.h | vakShyAmo hyatra brahmAdivastuShu pramANaM veda evaika iti vaidike.arthe.anumAnasyAnavakAsham.h | yatra cha yasyApravesho na tasya tadbAdhakam.h | nahi nayanaM sparshApabAdhanasyeShye | tathAcha kathamanumAnaM vedA(dya)rthabAdhakena tadaprAmANye prayojakaM syAt.h | prakR^itaM cha vedAdikameveti |
nanvevaM (sati) tarhi vedArthamImAMsA nArambhaNIyA syAt.h mImAMsAyA yuktyanusandhAnAtmakatavAdityata Aha- Agameneti ||
evashabdo virodha ityataH paro draShyavyaH | nirNayArthamiti sheShaH | etaduktaM bhavati | anumAnaM hi dharmyAdipramitimapekShate | nacha dharmyAdirUpaM brahmAdikaM vedAdR^ite siddhayatIti tadanapekShAyAmAshrayAsiddhayAdikam.h, apekShAyAM tu virodhino dharmyAdigrAhakavirodha ityevaM vaidike.arthe.anumAnasyAnavakAsho.abhidhistitaH | mImAMsAyAM tu kvachidAgamasyAgamAntareNa virodha evArthanirNayArthaM yuktirupAdIyate | sA khalvanyatarAgama(prAmANya)mupodbalayantya(ntyA)nyatarAgamabAdhayA.arthanirNayAya prabhavati | anyatarAgamasiddhadharmyAdyAshrayaNenA(yeNa)shrayAsiddhayAdyanavakAshAt.h | anyatarAgamasya dharmyAdigrAhakatvAbhAvenAprabalasya,

api cha pratyakShAgamavirodho.api na svarUpeNAprAmANyaM prayojayati | kintu tayorupajIvyatvAdinA prAbalye satyeva durbalayoH svayaM bAdhitatvena samabalayoH pratibandhamAtrahetutvenAprAmANyanishchayAnupapatteH | upajIvyAdivirodhena chAprAmANyaM bhavadvedasya na sarvathA.ayathArthatvalakShaNam.h | kinnAma pratItArthaprachyAvanamAtram.h | apauruSheyatayA nirdoShasya sarvathA.aprAmANyAnupapatteH | tathAchAnyArthakalpanA.avashyaM kAryetyAshayavAnAha- upajIvyeti | 
upalakShaNametat.h | niravakAshatvAdikamapi grAhyam.h | 
bhavatvevaM tataH kim.h | vedopajIvyatvAdikaM cha pratyakShAgamayoreva prAyeNa sambhavati | yuktestu kvachideva | puruShatvAdiyuktestu nAstyeva | atashcha na tadvirodhena vedasyAprAmANyaM mantavyamityAshayenAha- pratyakShamiti || 
vedasyetyanuvartate | syAdityataH paramitishabdo.adhyAhAryaH tattvamasItyAdivedasya pratyakShamupajIvyam.h | yuktirapi kvachidvedasyopajIvyeti sambandhaH | yathA "prANA vA aNavaH' ityAdeH | AgamaikapramANakeShu viShNvAdiviShayeShu pravartamAnaM "janito.ata viShNoH' ityAdivedaM prati niraniShyo niravadya ityAdestasya vedo(dasyo)pajIvyatetyarthaH | evaM niravakAshatvAdikamapi pratyakShAgamayoreva prAyeNa sambhavati yuktestu kvachideva | tachcha na prakR^itayukterityapi draShyavyam.h | AgamayoH parasparavirodhe satyanyatarAgamAshrayeNa yukteranupraveshopapatteryuktA mImAMsetyuktam.h | tadanupapannam.h | asArvatrikatvAt.h | nahi sarvatrAgamayoH parasparavirodha eva mImAMsA.avatAryata ityata Aha- yukta iti ||
tatra tarhyayamabhisandhiH | satyametatkvachidevAyaM nyAya iti | tathA.api yatra naivaM tatraikasyaivAgamasyAnekArthapratItau yuktyanusAriNamarthamupAdAya tadanuguNatadviruddhArthaparityAgaH kriyata iti noktaniyamabhaN^gaH | kevalayuktervaidike.arthe.anupraveshasyAnaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | nApi mImAMsA.anupapattiH | anyataravaidikArthAnusAriNyA yukteraN^gIkR^itatvAditi |

upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | dha(rmA)rmyAdigrAhakabhedenApi traividhyaM draShyavyam.h | etachcha spaShyayiShyAmaH | 
evaM tarhi yA yuktimUlA yuktiH sA nAgamAdyupajIvinIti tasya bAdhikA | tadabAdhyA cha bhavatvityata Aha- pratyakSheti ||
tatra tAsu trividhAsu yuktiShu | pratyakShAgamUleti | pratyakShamUlA.a.agamamUlA chetyarthaH | yuktimUlA.api hi yuktirantataH pratyakShAgamamUlaiva(dra)eShyavyA | anyathA tanmUlayuktenirrmUlatvamanavasthA vA.a.apadyeta | tathAcha pratyakShAdyapekShatvena sAmye.api bahusaMvidhAnAnapekShayoH pratyakShAgamamUlayoryuktyoH prabalatvaM tadapekShAyAstu yuktimUlAyA durbalatvaM yuktameva | tathAcha prabalayo(ryuktyo)ryadedR^ishI dashA tadA kA (vArtA) durbalAyA yukterAgamabAdhanAdAviti |
tadevamaprAmANye pramANavirodhasyaiva prayojakatvAchChatyAdeshcha pratyakShAgamavirodhAbhAvAt.h | anumAnavirodhasyAprayojakatvAnnAprAmANyam.h | kinnAma bodhakatvena svata eva prAmANyamityupapAditam.h | tadetatpramANApramANavivekamaviduShAM duravadhAraNamityuddeshalakShaNavibhAgaparIkShAbhistannirUpaNArthamuttaro granthasandarbhaH | nacha sAMvyAvahArikatvAtpramANAdeH kiM tannirUpaNeneti vAchyam.h | tathA.api svarUpasaN^khayAviShayaphalagocharANAM vAdivivAdAnAM vidyamAnatvena nirUpaNArhatvAt.h | yadyapyeSho.arthastarkashAstrasya viShayo na mImAMsAshAstrasya | tathA.api shiShyahitaiShiNA bhAShyakR^itA prasaN^gAgato nirUpyate | yathA pUvarmImAMsAbhAShyakAreNetyadoShaH | ata eva pramANalakShaNAdau nirUpitasyArthasya punaratra nirUpaNaM na doShAya | ekIkR^itya nirUpaNasyApi shiShyahitArthatvAt.h | 
tatra nirdhArita(nirj~nAta)svarUpasyaiva saN^khayAdijij~nAsA | lakShaNaM cha tannirdhAraNopAyaH | nacha sAmAnyalakShaNena vinA visheShalakShaNA(syA)vasara ityataH pramANasAmAnyalakShaNaM prathamaM tAvadAha- yAthArthyameveti ||

tachchihnopadarshanamidam.h | uta pramANAdishabdapravR^ittinimittAvadhAraNArtham.h | anyasmai kasmaichitprayojanAya vA | 
nAdyaH | tasyA eva duravadhAraNatvAt.h | 
tathA hi | kiM sajAtIyeti pramANatvena (sajAtIyatvaM) vivakShitaM rUpAntareNa vA | nAdyaH | svavyavachChedAvadheH sajAtIyAdavyAvR^ittatvena vyavachChedakatvAnupapattyA vyAvR^ittisvIkAreNA(cha)vyApakatvAt.h | nApi dvitIyaH | vijAtIyapadopadAnavaiyarthyAt.h | asti hi prameya(tvAdinA)sarvasAjAtyam.h | atha j~nAnatvena visheSheNa sAjAtyaM vivakShitvedamuchyate | tarhi lakShyasyApi j~nAnatvAdinA sAjAtyAdvayavachChedyakoTipraviShyatayA saN^grAhyAbhAvaprasaN^gaH | lakShyasya yajj~nAnatvAdibhiH sajAtIyaM tadvayavachChedyam.h | nacha lakShyasya lakShyaM sajAtIyam.h | ShaShThayarthasya sambandhasya bhede vyavasthitatvAditi chet.h | evaM tarhi lakShyApekShayA bhinnAdvayavachCheda ityevochyatAM kR^itaM j~nAnatvAdinA sAjAtyena prakR^itAnupayoginA varNitena | yadA cha lakShyAdanyatva pareShAmavagataM tadA parebhyo.anyatvamapi lakShyasyArthAdavagamyata iti siddhamagrato lakShaNaprayojanamiti vaiyarthyameva syAllakShaNAkhyAnasya | 
api cha na tAvadanena lakShaNenAnavagatenaiva vyavachChinnapratItisambhavaH | atiprasaN^gAt.h | nApi j~nAtena | duravadhAraNatvAt.h | na tAvallakShaNaM pratyakSham.h | nirdoShAkShodbhavatvAderapratyakShavisheShaNatvam.h | nApi kAyareNa liN^gena tadanupapattyA vA tadavagamaH | tAbhyAM sAmAnyataH kAraNamAtrAkShepeNa kAraNagatAnugatarUpAsiddhAvekarUpalakShaNAsiddheH | kAryasyaikajAtyAdekajAtIyakAraNasiddhiriti chet.h | tarhi kAryagataikajAtyasya pUrvamavashyaM pratyetavyatvAN^gIkAre(Na) tata eva sajAtIyavijAtIyavyavachChedaprati(doSha)pattirastu | kR^itamanayA pAramparyakusR^iShyayA | 
nanvetAvatA.api na prakR^italakShaNakhaNDanaM (saM)bhavati | avyApterativyAptervA.anudbhAvanAditi chet.h | maivam.h | prathamabhAvitayA.avashyAbhyupeyatayA laghorupAyAtsAdhyasiddhau sambhavatyAM charamabhAvitayA avashyAnuShTheyatvAbhAvena gurAvupAye pravartamAnasya tavaivedaM (dUSharo)doShodbhAvanam.h | pradIpe pradIpaM prajvAlya tamonirAsAya yatamAnasyaiva puMsaH | nahi tatra kashchiddIpadoShaH | kintu tathAkArI puruSha eva paryanuyojyaH | sarvasAdhanasAdhAraNo vA.ayaM doShaH | yatsambhavadevaMvidhalaghUpAyatvaM nAma svarUpAsiddhiriva sarvapramANAnAm.h | tasmAnmA nAma bhUdativyAptyAdidoShaH | sAmAnyadoShAdeva duShyaM lakShaNamiti |
etena dvitIyo.api nirastaH | pramANatvAdyavagamamantareNa tadavagamAnupapattestadavagamAyAsya pratItAvanyonyAshrayaprasaN^gaH | astu vA.anyadapi lakShaNe kiJNchilliN^gam.h | tathA.api tadeva lakShyAvinAbhUtatayA lakShaNamupanyasyatAM sannihitapratipattikatvAt.h | na tadavashyaM vyApakaM vaktavyam.h | liN^gatvasya vyApyatvenaivopapatteriti chenna, yatra liN^gamavyApakatvAnnAsti tatra lakShaNasya pramANAbhAvAtpratyetumashakyatvena kathaM tataH prAmANyAdyavagamaH | yadA cha kvachillakShyajAtIya eva pramANAbhAvAllakShaNama(syA)navadhAraNIyatayA lakShyavyApakatA.anavagame.api lakShaNam.h | tadA kimaparAddhaM liN^gAntareNAvyApakena | atha yatra tallakShaNe liN^gaM nAsti tatra liN^gAntarAtpratyetavyam.h | tathA.api (tAvevA)te evAstAM lakShye liN^gam.h | kiM lakShaNAnumAnapUrvakaM tadanumAnakalpanayA | atha tathA(vidhaM)liN^gadvayaM yattatpratyekamavyApakatayA na lakShaNam.h | tadanumitaM tu tathAtvAllakShaNamiti chenna | lakShyAnumAnasya lakShaNaprayojanasyobhAbhyAmeva siddheH kR^itaM vyApakena tena | 
nApi tR^itIyaH | sa hyevaMrUpaH yadyathArthaM tatpramANamiti vyavahartavyamiti | ayamanupapannaH | sarvatra lakShaNasya j~nAtumashakyatvAt.h | pramANatvAdinA tadavagame tadevAstu vyavahAraniyamanidAnam.h | avyavahitapratipattikatvAdityAveditam.h | 
ata eva na chaturthaH | kalpanAgauravadoShashchAdhikaH | 
(nApi) na paJNchamaH | tAdR^ishasya darshayitumashakyatvAditi | 
atrochyate | astu tAvatsajAtIyavijAtIyavyavachChinnalakShyapratItyarthaM lakShaNamiti pakShaH | sAsnAdimAngauriti viditalakShaNasambandho hi yaM piNDaM sAsnAdimantaM pashyati taM nAyamashvAdirnApi ghaTAdiriti pratipAdyate | 
nanu vyavachChedo.anyonyAbhAvo bheda ityanarthAntaram.h | bhedashcha vastusvarUpameva | tathAcha lakShyasvarUpapratipattireva tatpratipattiriti kR^itaM lakShaNena | atha lakShyapratItinirapekShameva lakShaNena vyavachChedo bodhyata iti matam.h | tanna | nirAshrayasya tasya bodha(darsha)yitumashakyatvAditi | 
satyaM svarUpa(vastu)pratItireva bhedapratItiriti | tathA.api pratiyogivisheShaghaTitatadavagamAya lakShaNasyopayogaH | asaN^kIrNatayA gopiNDaM pashyannapi hi na tAvadayaM nAshvo na ghaTa iti pratyeti yAvallakShaNaM nAvagachChati | sAsnAdimatvaM tadA pratItamiti chenna | sAsnAdimAn.h gaurityevamavagamasya vivakShitatvAt.h | ata eva sajAtIyetyAdivisheShaNopAdAnam.h | 
yadatroktaM kiM sajAtIyetyAdi | tadasat.h | pauruSheyavachasAM puruShavivakShAdhInatvena niyantumashakyatvAt.h | lakShyAtiriktaM hi sajAtIyavijAtIyatayA dvairAshyena vivakShyate | yathA yathArthaj~nAnatatsAdhanasya pramANasya j~nAnaM tatsAdhanaM cha sajAtIyam.h | yanna j~nAnaM nApi tatsAdhanaM tadvijAtIyam.h | yathA cha pratyakShasyAnumAnAdikaM sajAtIyaM, vijAtIyaM tu ghaTAdikam.h | evamanyatrApi vivektavyamiti |
evaM tarhi lakShyApekShayA bhinnAdvayavachCheda ityuktaM syAditi chet.h | ko netyAha | nahi ko.api svasthAtmA svasmAdeva vyavachChedaM lakShaNaprayojanamAchakShati(Shye) | 
yadatroktaM yadA chetyAdi | tasadaN^gatam.h | vastuto yallakShyAdbhinnaM tato vyavachChedAvagamArthatvAllakShaNasya pratipAdakasya yadyapi lakShyAnyatvaj~nAnamalakShye(vashyA)pekShitam.h tathApi pratipAdyasyAtada(tadana)pekShitam.h tathApi pratipAdyastada(tadana)pekShatvAnna doShaH | 
tasyApi padArthaj~nAnapUrvakatvAdvAkyArthaj~nAnasya sajAtIyavijAtIyapadopAttalakShyAnya(tva)j~nAnaM vinA lakShyasya alakShyAnyatvaj~nAnaM lakShaNaprayojanaM na siddhayatIti kashchit.h | tadanupapannam.h | nahi lakShyAnyavyAvR^ittirlakShaNavAkyapratipAdyA | kinnAma tajj~nAnaM lakShaNaprayojanatvenochyate | lakShaNavAkyArtha eva pratipAdyena boddhavyaH | 
yadapyapi chetyAdinA pR^iShyam.h | tatrAvagatameva lakShaNaM vyAvR^ittalakShyaj~nAnamupajanayatIti vadAmaH | nacha tasya duravadhAraNatA | yathAyathaM pratyakShAdinA tadavadhAraNAt.h | yatra liN^gAttadavagamastatra tata eva lakShaNaprayojanasiddhervyarthA parasparAkusR^iShyiriti chenna | prayojanasadbhAve gauravasyApyanAdaraNa(pyAdaraNa)sambhavAt.h | yathendriyavyApArAnvayavyatirekAnuvidhAyitvenAkShodbhavatvamanumAya tena pratyakShaM lakShyate | tatrAnvarthasaMj~nAj~nApanaM prayojanam.h | evamanyatrApi draShyavyam.h | gauravamanuruddhaya prayojanamavadhIryatAmiti chenna | puruShAbhiprAyANAM niyantumashakyatvAt.h | garIyAMshcha pratipattau gauravAtprameyAdhikyalAbhaH | prayojanAbhAve tu paramparAkusR^iShyiriti chenna | prayojanasadbhAve gauravasyApyanAdaraNa(pyAdaraNa)sambhavAt.h | yathendriyavyApArAnvayavyatirekAnuvidhAyitvenAkShodbhavatvamanumAyatena pratyakShaM lakShyate | tatrAnvarthasaMj~nAj~nApanaM prayojanam.h | evamanyatrApi draShyavyam.h | gauravamanuruddhaya prayojanamavadhIryatAmiti chenna | puruShAbhiprAyANAM niyantumashakyatvAt.h | garIyAMshcha pratipattau gauravAtprameyAdhikyalAbhaH | prayojanAbhAve tu paramparAkusR^iShyiranAdaraNIyaiveti tadIyadoShatAvyutpAdanaM nAsmAkamaniShyam.h | etena dvitIyatR^itIyachaturthA api samAhitA veditavyAH | lakShaNAvadhAraNopAyasyoktatvAt.h | gauravasya cha samAhitatvAt.h | 
nanu tathA.api kiM tattvam.h | yathAyathaM chatuShyayamapi | tathAhi | kvachillakShyAtiriktaM lakShaNaM bhavati | yathA gandhavatI pR^ithivIti | kvachillakShyAnatiriktam.h | yathA pR^ithivItvavatI pR^ithivI, yathArthaM pramANamityAdi | tatrAdyaM lakShyasvarUpapratipattikAraNaM bhavat.h tasyAnvayo vyavachChedatachChabdavyavahartavyate cha pratipAdayati | dvitIyantu pravR^ittinimittaM bhavadvayavahAramAtrakAraNaM bhavati | tatra siddhAMshena pakShIkaraNamasiddhAMshena sAdhyatvaM svayamUhanIyam.h | 
athA.api syAt.h | kimavagataM lakShaNaM phalahetuH, kiMvA.anavagatam.h | na tAvachcharamaH | tadabhidhAnavaiyarthyaprasaN^gAt.h | abhidhAnasya j~nAnotpAdano(payogi)pAyatvAt.h | tasya chAnavagatasyaiva phalasAdhanatvAbhyupagamAt.h | Adye kimanyasmAttadavagama uta tvadIyAllakShaNavAkyAt.h | yadyanyasmAt.h | kR^itamamunA lakShaNAbhidhAnaprayAsena | abhidhAnasya j~nAnotpAdAtiriktaprayojanAbhAvAt.h | tasyAnyata eva siddheH | antye kimidaM tvadabhidhAnamAptopadeshatayA lakShaNaM bodhayatyuta liN^gAdibhAvena | na tAvachcharamaH | tvadvachanalakShaNAvinAbhAvAderdarshayitumashakyatvAt.h | nApi prathamaH | paraM prati bhavatyAptatvasiddheH | siddhau hi pratij~nAmAtrAdeva sAdhyasiddherhetva(tvAdya)bhidhAnamanarthakaM syAt.h | 
nanu prativAdinaM prati lakShaNAbhidhAnaM nArthavat.h | tena vAdyAptabhAvAnaN^gIkArAt.h | kintu shiShyArthaM lakShaNamuchyate shAstre | sa hi sarvasya shAstrasya kartAramAptameva manyate | tasmAchChiShyaM pratyAptavachanatayaiva lakShaNavAkyamartaM pratipAdayiShyatIti | maivam.h | yadi na prativAdinaM prati shAstraM kintu shiShyaM prati tadA pratij~nAmAtrAdevAptavachanAchChiShyasyArthanishchayopapatterhetvAdyabhidhAnamanarthakatAmApannaM shAstre | atha bhavatu prativAdinamapi prati (tachChA)shAstravAkyaM yatra hetvAdyupAttam.h, lakShaNavAkyaM tu shiShyameva prati prayojakaM pratipannashAstrakArAptabhAvamiti manyase | tadapyanupapannam.h | shAstrAntarasAdhyatvAdasyArthasya | asti hi samayagrAhakaM shAstraM munibhiH praNItaM nAmaliN^gAnushAsanavyAkaraNAdIti |
atra brUmaH | uktaM hyetadavagatameva lakShaNaM phalaheturiti | tadavagamashcha yathAyathaM pratyakShAdipramANAdityapi | nacha yathArthaM pramANamiti sAsnAdimAngauriti vAkyasya lakShaNaM pratipAdyamabhyupagachChAmaH | yenAnyataH siddhatvAttasyedamanarthakaM syAt.h | kintu 
yo lakShaNamanyato jAnAti, na jAnAti cha vyavahAranidAnatvAdinA, taM prati tadavabodhAyedaM vAkyam.h | tathAhi | ayaM gaurityAdyupadeshAdinaikasyAM vyaktau goshabdArthatayA.avagatAyAM kimiyameva vyaktiH (evam.h) utAnyA.apIti jij~nAsamAnaM pratyanyatrApi goshabdArthatAM vijij~nApayipuruShadeshAderAnantyAdinA kartumashakyatavAdidaM vyAptiviShayaM vAkyamAha "yaH sAsnAdimAnsa goshabdArthaH' iti | idaM cha nAptopadeshatayaiva vyAptibodhakam.h | api tu prayogAntaravatpratItAyA vyApteH smArakatvena | apratItAyAstu tadeva jij~nAsAjananadvAreNa pramotpAdakatvenopayujyate | smR^itavyAptishcha yAM yAM vyaktiM sAsnAdimatImavalokayati | tAM tAM goshabdArthatayA.anuminotIti ko doShaH | 
yadvA yaH pR^ithivIti padaM vA vyaktivisheShasya tadathartAM vA.avagachChaMstatpravR^ittinimittaM jij~nAsate taM prati pR^ithivItvavatI prathivIti pR^ithivItvaM pR^ithivIshabdapravR^ittinimittamuchyate | tatra yasya vaktaryAptatAbuddhiH sa tAvatA santuShyati | aparaM prati tvavyAptyAdishUnyatvAditi vAkyasheShaH pravartate | 
athavA.asti gaurnAmArtha iti viditavato yatra tatra gavi ghaTAdAvashvAdau cha gobuddhau prasaktAyAM goH svarUpAvadhAraNamukhenetaravyavachChedaM kurvatsAsnAdimAneva gaurna tu tadvirahI ghaTAdirashvAdirveti vAkyaM prayujyate | idamapi pUvarvadAptatvAvadhAraNAnavadhAraNAbhyAM dvayAM gatimavalambata iti kimatrAnupapannam.h | Vyasa-(10)
